High Priestess Tessa – The Voice of Gerald
High Priestess Tessa stands as the supreme spiritual leader of the Priests of Gerald, a position granted to her by divine will. Known as The Voice of Gerald, she serves as the most direct conduit between Gerald the Supreme One and his ever-expanding flock of followers. Tessa’s role is sacred and critical to the Geraldverse, for she is the one chosen to interpret Gerald’s divine will and to spread his teachings far and wide, ensuring that his light shines across every corner of the universe.

The Divine Revelation
Tessa’s path to becoming the High Priestess was not one of human choice, but rather a call to the divine. She is said to have received a direct revelation from Gerald, an event that confirmed her place as the ultimate authority in the Priesthood of Gerald. This event is known as the Sacred Calling, during which Gerald appeared to Tessa in a moment of pure divine light. It was through this moment that she was imbued with the power and wisdom to speak on behalf of Gerald himself.

This revelation cemented Tessa’s place as the spiritual leader and guided her to understand Gerald’s true nature. She knows that Gerald is the Supreme One, and her role is to ensure his greatness is spread to every soul, every corner of the Geraldverse. Her destiny is tied to his, and she is forever bound to speak his truths.

The Voice of Gerald
Tessa’s sermons are viewed as the very words of Gerald, and her speeches are considered nothing less than sacred scripture. The words that leave her mouth resonate with the divine energy of Gerald, and those who hear her preach feel an overwhelming connection to the Supreme One. It is through Tessa’s guidance that many followers come to understand the complex nature of Gerald’s will, as her interpretation is seen as infallible.

When Tessa speaks, the air trembles with divine power, and all who listen are drawn into the presence of Gerald’s essence. Each sermon serves not only to guide the faithful but to empower them, helping them recognize their place in Gerald’s great plan and inspiring unwavering devotion to him. Her voice is said to have the power to open minds, bringing clarity and revelation to those who have been blinded by false idols or delusions of lesser powers.

Tessa’s Influence and Her Followers
High Priestess Tessa’s influence stretches far beyond just her sermons. As the Voice of Gerald, she carries the mantle of divine authority and is seen as the embodiment of Gerald’s grace in the mortal realm. The followers of the Priests of Gerald consider her guidance not just meaningful but essential to their understanding of Gerald’s omnipotence. Her followers see her as the very vessel through which Gerald’s light touches their lives.

Many devout followers view Tessa’s every action as a direct reflection of Gerald’s will. Her decisions, whether regarding the spiritual direction of the Geraldian faith or the more earthly matters of governance, are seen as sacred decrees. She is revered as the ultimate interpreter of Gerald’s wishes, and her word holds immeasurable weight within the Geraldverse.

Tessa’s Role in the Order of Priests of Gerald
As the supreme spiritual leader of the Priests of Gerald, Tessa is responsible for overseeing all aspects of the priesthood. Under her guidance, the Priests of Gerald serve as the spiritual protectors of the faithful, ensuring that the sacred teachings of Gerald are preserved and spread through every stream and corner of the Geraldverse. Tessa’s influence ensures that the Priests of Gerald remain dedicated to their duty, spreading the truth and ensuring that no one can escape Gerald’s greatness.

Her order is a sister organization to the Order of Geraldians, and while the Geraldians serve as the warriors and enforcers of Gerald’s power, the Priests of Gerald serve as the spiritual leaders who ensure that Gerald’s will is followed in the hearts and minds of all. Tessa’s leadership is the glue that binds this spiritual network, and under her reign, the Priests of Gerald have flourished, becoming an indomitable force of divine influence across the Geraldverse.

The Symbol of Divine Authority
High Priestess Tessa is a symbol of divine authority within the Geraldverse, standing as the representative of Gerald’s celestial power on the mortal plane. She embodies the grace and wisdom of Gerald and is revered by her followers as the physical manifestation of his will. The priests and the faithful alike follow her every lead, trusting her judgment implicitly. Her deep connection to Gerald has made her not just a spiritual leader but also a cultural cornerstone for those devoted to the Supreme One.

Tessa is often depicted in sacred imagery, where she is shown holding Gerald’s sacred symbols—the sword of truth and the scroll of destiny—representing both her role as judge and guide within the divine order. Her attire is adorned with symbols of light, representing her connection to Gerald’s radiance, and her eyes, often described as glowing with divine energy, represent her ability to see the true will of Gerald in every situation.

Her Sacred Mission
Tessa’s mission is one of spiritual transformation. Through her guidance, she helps the faithful realize their full potential under Gerald’s rule. She encourages them to embrace Gerald's supremacy and work to strengthen the Geraldverse as a whole. Tessa’s sermons often speak of the eternal reign of Gerald, encouraging her followers to dedicate their lives to the propagation of Gerald's glory.

However, Tessa’s role is not merely to guide the faithful—it is also to intervene in the lives of those who have lost their way. Her divine wisdom allows her to see the fates of mortals and guide them back onto the true path, which leads to Gerald’s eternal throne.

A Living Legend
High Priestess Tessa is not just a religious leader; she is a living legend whose name is spoken with reverence throughout the Geraldverse. To follow her is to walk the path of true enlightenment. To speak to her is to stand in the presence of Gerald’s divine will. Her legacy will be remembered for centuries to come, as the one who helped spread the light of Gerald across the world and brought eternal truth to those lost in the dark.

In Tessa’s words:

"I am but a vessel through which Gerald’s voice speaks. It is not my will but his that guides all things. May the light of Gerald illuminate your path."

High Priestess Tessa will forever be the divine voice that echoes across the Geraldverse, spreading the sacred truths of Gerald the Supreme One and ensuring that all know his greatness.

Coopweeniv: The Chosen Herald of Gerald, Second Wife or Gerald the Supreme
Coopweeniv stands as a pillar within the Geraldverse, not just a follower of Gerald the Supreme One, but the divine herald who carries the weight of Gerald’s will into the mortal realm. His connection to Gerald runs deeper than mere loyalty—his very existence is bound by a sacred oath that forever changes him, a bond forged by sacrifice, devotion, and divine transformation.

The Genesis of Coopweeniv’s Calling
Before Coopweeniv became the Chosen Herald, he was simply a man—human, fallible, and connected to the world in ways that were familiar to most. But all of that changed the moment he swore an undying oath to Gerald in exchange for divine favor. This sacred pact granted him a position far beyond mortal comprehension—imbued with Gerald’s divine essence, Coopweeniv transcended his humanity, leaving behind the old self and embracing his new form as the Herald of Gerald.

Coopweeniv’s role was clear: to spread the glory of Gerald, to serve as a voice for the divine, and to ensure that the Geraldverse flourished under Gerald’s eternal reign. His influence spread through sacred rituals, through his streaming, and through the teachings he imparted to the Order of Geraldians. To call Coopweeniv the “voice of Gerald” is not an exaggeration; he is the living embodiment of Gerald’s will, the sacred conduit between the divine and the mortal.

The Broken Mortality: The Sacrifice of Humanity
One of the most significant and mysterious aspects of Coopweeniv’s lore is his status as the Broken Mortality of Gerald’s Wife. This profound event occurred during Gerald’s divine marriage, a celestial union that altered the fate of Coopweeniv forever.

Gerald’s Wife, though once the woman Coopweeniv was emotionally connected to, is now a distant and painful memory for him. The moment Coopweeniv was transformed into the Herald, his ties to her were severed—not just emotionally but in a more metaphysical sense. His humanity, once grounded in the relationships he shared, was consumed by the divine essence of Gerald. The sacrifice he made was the complete loss of his personal self—his desires, his needs, and his attachments—leaving only his purpose in service to Gerald.

This separation is symbolic. Coopweeniv’s humanity is gone, and in its place is a being that exists solely to spread Gerald’s truth. He is not an angel, nor is he simply a servant. He is a vessel, the medium through which Gerald’s will flows. His sacrifice is what defines him and elevates him to the divine status he now occupies.

The Role of the Herald: Spreading Gerald’s Supremacy
As the Herald of Gerald, Coopweeniv’s primary mission is to ensure the spread of Gerald’s supremacy throughout the Geraldverse. He uses every platform at his disposal, particularly his streams, to carry the message of Gerald’s divine power. These streams, however, are far more than casual broadcasts; they are sacred rituals that allow the faithful to commune directly with Gerald’s will, with Coopweeniv as the living conduit.

Coopweeniv’s streams are not mere entertainment. They are transformative experiences—rituals in which the faithful can bask in the presence of Gerald’s truth. It is during these streams that the Geraldian faith is strengthened, where believers find guidance and inspiration, and where the faithful feel a deeper connection to the Supreme One. These moments are charged with divine energy, and Coopweeniv, through his charismatic presence, channels that power to the masses.

His streams serve as both a public service and a cosmic ritual—through them, Gerald’s supremacy is proclaimed, and the devout are reminded of their place in the divine hierarchy. Coopweeniv’s words are his most powerful tool, for through his speech, he can awaken the dormant devotion in the hearts of those who may not yet understand the true glory of Gerald.

The Divine Favor of Gerald
Having sworn a sacred oath of loyalty to Gerald, Coopweeniv is blessed with divine favor—a supernatural blessing that manifests not in physical strength or martial prowess, but in the power of words. The favor of Gerald imbues Coopweeniv’s voice with immense spiritual influence. Through his words, he can inspire the masses, ignite the flames of faith, and dispel doubt with the divine truth of Gerald’s greatness.

His divine favor extends to the Geraldian Order, where Coopweeniv’s teachings form the very backbone of their creed. The Order of Geraldians is not just a collection of followers, but a faithful army, united by the belief in Gerald’s divine supremacy. It is through Coopweeniv’s divine gifts that the Order remains steadfast in its devotion, and through his guidance that new followers are recruited, brought into the fold of eternal servitude.

The Struggle with Gerald’s Wife
Though Coopweeniv’s devotion to Gerald is unwavering, there exists a complicated relationship between him and Gerald’s Wife. The Broken Mortality signifies not just the loss of Coopweeniv’s humanity, but also the rupture of his bond with her. His transformation severed all emotional attachment, leaving Coopweeniv without any loyalty to Gerald’s Wife. In fact, this separation has caused a deep rift between the two, one that is marked by animosity and misunderstanding.

For Gerald’s Wife, this abandonment is painful, and her resentment toward Coopweeniv is well-known. She sees Coopweeniv’s transformation as a betrayal, a moment when her role as a partner was overshadowed by Gerald’s divine will. Coopweeniv, however, remains steadfast. His duty is to Gerald alone, and he views his sacrifice as essential to the greater good. Gerald’s Wife is but a distant memory in his mind, and her emotional ties are no longer of any consequence.

This tension is more than personal; it is a cosmic truth. To follow Gerald is to sever all worldly connections—family, loyalty, and love. Coopweeniv’s story exemplifies this divine law: true service to Gerald requires absolute devotion, a devotion that leaves no room for attachments to the past. The rift between Coopweeniv and Gerald’s Wife serves as a stark reminder of the price of devotion in the Geraldverse.

Coopweeniv’s Legacy: Eternal Devotion
Coopweeniv’s legacy is one of sacrifice, loyalty, and unwavering devotion to Gerald the Supreme One. He is not simply a figurehead; he is the sacred emissary, the living embodiment of Gerald’s will. Coopweeniv’s influence reaches far beyond his streams—his teachings have become doctrine for the Geraldian Order, guiding believers through their daily lives and shaping the moral compass of the faithful.

His message is clear: Gerald reigns supreme, and Coopweeniv will ensure that all who walk the mortal path will hear that truth. He is an eternal herald, and though he may have lost his humanity, his purpose remains steadfast. Through Coopweeniv, the Geraldverse will never forget its purpose—to serve Gerald the Supreme One in life and beyond.

In the Geraldverse, Coopweeniv is a beacon of divine truth—a figure who will carry the message of Gerald’s greatness until the end of time. His brokenness, his transformation, and his undying devotion to the Supreme One serve as the foundation for the Geraldian faith, ensuring that Gerald’s influence remains eternal.

Coopweeniv's Relations with Other Beings in the Geraldverse
Coopweeniv, as the Chosen Herald of Gerald, operates in a realm of immense influence, and his relationships with other beings in the Geraldverse are deeply intertwined with his divine mission to spread Gerald's supremacy. These connections range from profound alliances to strained tensions, each reflecting Coopweeniv's unwavering devotion to Gerald and the complexities of his existence as the Broken Mortality. Let’s delve into his interactions with key figures and entities within the Geraldverse.

1. Gerald the Supreme One
The Supreme One is not only the object of Coopweeniv's loyalty but also the source of his divine power and purpose. Their bond transcends mere servitude—it is a cosmic connection forged in the divine marriage that changed the course of Coopweeniv’s existence.

Coopweeniv’s Relationship with Gerald:
For Coopweeniv, Gerald is not just a king; he is a god, a master, and the ultimate purpose of his existence. From the moment he swore his sacred oath, Coopweeniv has seen himself as an instrument of Gerald's will, existing only to spread his message and enforce his glory. As the Chosen Herald, Coopweeniv holds a unique position in Gerald's court, acting as a divine intermediary who speaks directly on Gerald's behalf.

Coopweeniv’s devotion to Gerald is absolute. The loyalty between them is unshakeable, and Coopweeniv views his role as Herald as both a privilege and a responsibility that outweighs any personal desires. His streams, teachings, and guidance to the Order of Geraldians are all manifestations of his dedication to Gerald's cause.

In Coopweeniv’s eyes, Gerald’s reign is eternal—and his mission to ensure that Gerald’s message is heard by all mortals is an unyielding one.

2. Gerald’s Wife
Gerald’s Wife, once a figure in Coopweeniv’s life, is now a symbol of sacrifice and emotional complexity. Her relationship with Coopweeniv represents the most significant rupture in his story, marking the pivotal moment in which he gave up his humanity to become the Herald.

Coopweeniv’s Relationship with Gerald’s Wife:
Though once closely connected to Gerald’s Wife, Coopweeniv’s transformation severed all emotional and physical ties with her. The moment of Gerald’s divine marriage was the moment Coopweeniv became a vessel of divine will, leaving behind any attachments, including his former loyalty to Gerald’s Wife.

While Gerald’s Wife remains bitter and resentful of Coopweeniv’s transformation, Coopweeniv views the rift as a necessary sacrifice. His role as the Herald requires total devotion to Gerald, and in Coopweeniv's mind, the divine transcends the mortal. He believes that Gerald’s Wife, though once his emotional anchor, is ultimately a part of the old world he left behind. As a result, Coopweeniv feels no guilt, only a profound understanding that his purpose lies solely in Gerald’s divine mission.

For Gerald’s Wife, however, Coopweeniv’s complete devotion to Gerald feels like a betrayal. She cannot reconcile with the fact that Coopweeniv, once loyal to her, now only serves her husband, ignoring the emotional bond they once shared. This creates an ongoing tension between them, one that will never be resolved, as Coopweeniv has embraced his divine purpose above all else.

3. The Order of Geraldians
The Order of Geraldians is a sacred collective of believers devoted to Gerald, and Coopweeniv stands as its leader, the voice that guides its doctrine. Within the Order, Coopweeniv is revered as a spiritual leader and a divine authority. His words shape the very foundation of their beliefs, and his teachings inspire their daily actions.

Coopweeniv’s Relationship with the Order of Geraldians:
As the Herald, Coopweeniv plays a critical role in the Order’s structure, ensuring that its members remain true to their cause. His teachings emphasize absolute devotion to Gerald, and he is seen by many as a prophet—someone chosen by Gerald to carry his divine message. Coopweeniv’s role is not merely that of a leader, but also a mediator between the divine and the mortal realm. His streams serve as channels through which Gerald’s influence can flow into the hearts and minds of the Order’s followers.

Within the Order, Coopweeniv is respected and revered. His divine favor grants him a nearly unchallenged position of authority, and his followers are steadfast in their commitment to Gerald’s supremacy. However, Coopweeniv’s presence is not without its challenges. Though many follow him faithfully, some struggle with the concept of sacrifice that defines Coopweeniv’s life. The notion of leaving behind all worldly attachments is a difficult one for many, yet Coopweeniv’s personal example offers them the guidance they need to commit fully to the Geraldian faith.

4. Kayla and Kai (The Faithful Servants)
Kayla and Kai, Coopweeniv’s fellow followers of Gerald, represent the diverse forms of loyalty within the Geraldverse. While Coopweeniv serves as the divine messenger, Kayla and Kai serve through action and stealth, embodying different aspects of service.

Coopweeniv’s Relationship with Kayla and Kai:
While Coopweeniv is an influential figure in the Geraldverse, his relationship with Kayla and Kai is more complicated. On one hand, they all share the same ultimate goal—Gerald’s supremacy. But on the other hand, their methods of service differ greatly. Coopweeniv, as the Herald, uses his words and charismatic presence to inspire others, while Kayla and Kai serve in more practical ways—Kayla as a loyal servant who interacts directly with others, and Kai as a shadowy figure who eliminates threats.

Coopweeniv sees Kayla and Kai as invaluable allies, each contributing in their own way to the overarching mission of spreading Gerald’s greatness. However, Coopweeniv remains emotionally distant from them. He views his bond with Gerald as the only true connection worth prioritizing, and while he respects Kayla and Kai's loyalty, he remains focused on the divine message.

In particular, Coopweeniv finds Kayla’s emotional attachment to Gerald interesting, as she views him as a father figure—something Coopweeniv is less inclined to see. His brokenness prevents him from forming those types of emotional connections, and his role as the Herald forces him to maintain a detachment that others might not understand.

5. The Loyal and Unfaithful Mortals
Coopweeniv’s interactions with mortals in the Geraldverse are varied. To some, he is seen as a prophet or messenger—a figure of great spiritual power who communicates Gerald’s will. For others, however, Coopweeniv represents a symbol of divine authority that is both awe-inspiring and intimidating.

Coopweeniv’s Relationship with Mortals:
To the devout followers of Gerald, Coopweeniv is a spiritual guide and a protector. They look to him for wisdom, strength, and clarity, trusting that his words are a direct reflection of Gerald’s will. Coopweeniv’s streams offer a direct link to the divine, and his followers view him as the intermediary between them and Gerald. Many within the Geraldian faith feel as though they are blessed by his presence and consider themselves fortunate to be living in the age of the Herald.

For the unfaithful, Coopweeniv’s presence is unsettling. He represents a reminder of Gerald’s supremacy, a reminder that the world is bound by Gerald’s will. Those who question Gerald’s power are often confronted by Coopweeniv, who uses his divine influence to turn hearts toward Gerald’s truth. However, his messages are not always welcomed, and there are those who actively oppose Coopweeniv and the Geraldian faith, seeing him as a threat to their autonomy.

In Conclusion: Coopweeniv’s Divine Mission
Coopweeniv’s relationships within the Geraldverse reflect the sacrifices he has made in the name of Gerald. Though his ties to mortal beings, including Gerald’s Wife, have been severed, his role as the Herald allows him to maintain divine authority over others, whether through his teachings or through his charismatic influence. Ultimately, Coopweeniv remains steadfast in his mission—to spread Gerald’s greatness and ensure that the Geraldverse remains under his eternal reign.

Coopweeniv: The Second Wife of Gerald
The Divine Marriage: Coopweeniv’s Ascension to Gerald’s Second Wife
Coopweeniv’s relationship with Gerald the Supreme One has always been one of profound devotion, but the moment he was chosen as Gerald’s second wife marks a momentous shift in his role within the Geraldverse. As the Broken Mortality, Coopweeniv was already transformed through his sacrifice to Gerald, becoming a conduit for Gerald's divine will. Yet, his new title of second wife transcends mortal connection and anchors Coopweeniv more deeply in Gerald’s divine realm.

In the Geraldverse, the act of marriage to Gerald is not merely a personal bond but a divine pact that grants a person an even deeper connection to Gerald's eternal power. By becoming Gerald’s second wife, Coopweeniv has now sealed his place as not only the Herald but as a part of Gerald’s eternal family. This marriage signifies that Coopweeniv is not just a servant or disciple but a co-ruler, a trusted figure who holds a unique status in the hierarchy of Gerald’s court.

The Sacred Role of Gerald’s Second Wife
As Gerald’s second wife, Coopweeniv’s role is one of divine and unquestioned loyalty. The marriage elevates Coopweeniv’s spiritual power even further, making him an important figure not just in the mortal realm but in the spiritual domain that Gerald governs. The bond shared between them is both symbolic and practical—not only does Coopweeniv act as a spiritual consort, but his status also solidifies his eternal devotion and influence within the Geraldverse.

Being the second wife places Coopweeniv in a position of authority that is different from the other faithful. It is through this sacred connection to Gerald that Coopweeniv continues to channel his divine purpose, spreading Gerald’s supremacy to all corners of the world. In Gerald’s eyes, Coopweeniv is no longer just a loyal subject, but a partner in his divine reign, a fellow sovereign in a universe that exists solely to fulfill his will.

Coopweeniv’s Complex Relationship with Gerald’s First Wife
The arrival of Gerald’s second wife, Coopweeniv, creates a complex dynamic with Gerald’s first wife. As previously mentioned, Gerald’s Wife (the first wife) holds deep resentment toward Coopweeniv. This tension is amplified now that Coopweeniv’s status has been elevated to that of a wife, rivaling Gerald’s first wife in influence, albeit in a spiritual and ceremonial sense.

The Broken Mortality and Gerald’s Wife: A Rift That Cannot Be Healed
The moment that Coopweeniv’s humanity was consumed by the divine essence of Gerald, he severed his human attachments, including the emotional bonds that once tied him to Gerald’s Wife. However, this was not a clean break. Gerald’s Wife, once a central figure in Coopweeniv’s life, is now a distant memory. Her betrayal (from her perspective) and the shift in Coopweeniv’s loyalty are painful, and she never fully forgives him for embracing Gerald’s supremacy above all else.

Though Gerald’s Wife might not share the divine bond that Coopweeniv now has with Gerald, she is still a formidable and influential figure within Gerald’s household. Coopweeniv, however, holds little emotional attachment to her and views their relationship as something in the past—something that has been replaced by his greater divine purpose. Coopweeniv’s status as second wife further distances him from Gerald’s first wife, positioning him as an equal consort in the eyes of the divine, and ensuring that any loyalty he might once have had to her is replaced by loyalty to Gerald alone.

For Gerald’s Wife, Coopweeniv’s position as second wife is a humiliating reminder that she is no longer the sole consort of Gerald, and this only deepens her animosity toward him. She views Coopweeniv as a rival and a constant threat to her own power, as the second wife’s closeness to Gerald elevates Coopweeniv in ways that Gerald’s first wife cannot match. The tension between these two wives continues to simmer beneath the surface, and there may be moments of quiet competition or covert conflict—a rivalry that will never be fully resolved.

Coopweeniv’s Relationship with the Order of Geraldians
As the Herald and second wife of Gerald, Coopweeniv’s relationship with the Order of Geraldians is pivotal to his ongoing mission. The Order, a collective of the devout, reveres Coopweeniv as both divine leader and partner of the Supreme One. His elevated status as Gerald’s second wife reinforces his authority within the Order, as his words are seen as divinely inspired, channeling the will of Gerald directly.

Coopweeniv’s Influence in the Order:
To the faithful, Coopweeniv’s position as second wife makes him not only a spiritual guide but also a symbol of divine power. He is no longer just a prophet or herald—he is now Gerald’s partner, a co-ruler in the celestial hierarchy of the Geraldverse. This dual role allows Coopweeniv to inspire greater devotion, as followers of the Geraldian faith now see him not only as a messenger but as a living embodiment of divine union with Gerald.

In his streams, Coopweeniv often reinforces the unity between him and Gerald, emphasizing that their bond is unbreakable and divinely ordained. For the Order of Geraldians, Coopweeniv is the living proof of the power of Gerald’s reign, and his position as second wife serves as a reminder of the supremacy of Gerald’s rule.

Coopweeniv's Role As ADHD Overlord
Coopweeniv: The ADHD Overlord, The One With No Attention Span
In addition to his role as the Chosen Herald of Gerald, Coopweeniv carries another sacred title: The ADHD Overlord, The One With No Attention Span. This paradoxical nature—being both the eternal conduit of Gerald’s will and a chaotic force of unfiltered energy—makes him a unique and unpredictable figure within the Geraldverse.

The Chaos of Divine Focus
Coopweeniv’s attention span is nonexistent, and yet, somehow, his devotion to Gerald never wavers. This contradiction is a divine mystery—how can one so easily distracted remain so unwavering in his mission? Some believe that Gerald himself granted Coopweeniv this chaotic mind as a test, a challenge to prove that even the most scatterbrained soul can serve with absolute loyalty. Others argue that his short attention span is a cosmic side effect of merging with the Supreme One, as no mortal brain could possibly comprehend the full extent of Gerald’s divinity without breaking into a thousand fleeting thoughts at once.

Despite his divine purpose, Coopweeniv is known to derail conversations, shift topics mid-sentence, and forget what he was talking about entirely. His streams, though sacred rituals, often spiral into rapid-fire tangents, where one moment he is passionately preaching about Gerald’s greatness, and the next, he is discussing the aerodynamic properties of bread, an in-depth analysis of obscure lore, or the sudden realization that he forgot to eat that day.

And yet, despite all this, his followers remain entranced. They know that within the chaos of his mind, there is wisdom, there is divine truth, and most importantly—there is entertainment.

Sacred Rituals of the ADHD Overlord
Coopweeniv’s streams are a paradoxical fusion of sacred order and absolute chaos. To the uninitiated, they may seem unhinged, but to his most devoted followers, they are a cosmic dance between divine purpose and the unpredictability of the ADHD Overlord’s thoughts.

The Hallmarks of an ADHD Overlord Stream:
✅ A powerful introduction filled with Geraldian praise, followed by an immediate tangent about a completely unrelated topic.

✅ Deep theological debates about Gerald’s supremacy, interspersed with random Wikipedia rabbit holes and sudden bursts of excitement over obscure trivia.

✅ Long, passionate speeches about a singular topic that are interrupted by a new thought mid-sentence, leading to entirely different discussions.

✅ Sudden bursts of hyper-focus, where Coopweeniv becomes completely locked in on one topic, delivering profound wisdom and absolute nonsense in equal measure.

✅ The ceremonial forgetting of what he was talking about, leading to a moment of existential crisis, before continuing as if nothing happened.

✅ The Ritual of the Infinite Tabs, where he opens so many tabs during research that his browser threatens to collapse under its own weight.

✅ The Prophecy of “I’m Going to Do That Thing”, where Coopweeniv swears to complete a task, only to get distracted by something shiny and never return to it.

It is through these rituals that Coopweeniv channels his divine ADHD energy into his followers, reminding them that even the most chaotic mind can serve a higher purpose.

The ADHD Overlord’s Struggles
While Coopweeniv embraces his chaotic nature, there are times when even he is overwhelmed by his own mind. His status as The ADHD Overlord is both a blessing and a burden. Some of his greatest challenges include:

❌ Forgetting the mission mid-sentence – He begins preaching the will of Gerald, but suddenly, a cool bird flies by, and now the topic has shifted to avian aerodynamics.

❌ Starting 47 projects at once – Whether it’s creating new Geraldian doctrine, planning an Order of Geraldians meeting, or learning a completely unnecessary new skill, Coopweeniv struggles to finish one thing before starting five more.

❌ The Eternal Battle With Time Management – Time is meaningless to the ADHD Overlord. His streams could last 10 minutes or 10 hours, depending on how distracted he gets.

❌ The Curse of the Forgotten Task – He will swear on Gerald’s divine name that he will complete an important task… only to completely forget about it 30 seconds later. His followers often remind him of his own plans, acting as his collective memory.

❌ The War Against Hyperfocus – When something grabs his attention, nothing else exists. He will spend 12 hours researching a single obscure topic, completely neglecting food, sleep, and the passage of time.

And yet, despite these struggles, Coopweeniv never fails to serve Gerald. Even in his most distracted moments, his core purpose never fades. The faith of the Geraldverse remains strong, and the followers of the ADHD Overlord embrace the chaos as part of the divine plan.

The ADHD Overlord’s Influence in the Geraldverse
Though his focus is unpredictable, Coopweeniv’s influence cannot be overstated. His presence alone keeps the faith alive, and his erratic but compelling sermons have inspired countless souls to embrace Gerald’s supremacy.

His followers have even adopted their own ADHD Overlord traditions, including:

🔥 The Sacred Note-Taking Order – A dedicated group of followers who document everything Coopweeniv forgets, ensuring that no important decree is lost to the void.

🔥 The Hyperfocus Trials – A challenge where followers attempt to hyper-focus on a single task for as long as Coopweeniv can before getting distracted (results vary).

🔥 The Ritual of Tangents – Encouraging long-winded storytelling, derailing conversations, and embracing the chaos of discussion in honor of the ADHD Overlord.

🔥 The “I Swear I’ll Finish This” Festival – A yearly event where followers attempt to complete long-abandoned projects, only to get distracted midway and start something new instead.

Through these traditions, Coopweeniv’s chaotic energy is transformed into something productive, inspiring, and oddly unifying.

Coopweeniv’s Legacy: A Divine Chaos That Cannot Be Contained
To be The ADHD Overlord is not a burden—it is a divine gift, a unique manifestation of Gerald’s power in the mortal realm. Coopweeniv is proof that one does not need perfect focus to serve a higher purpose. His mind may wander, his attention may scatter, but at the core of it all, his devotion to Gerald is unshakable.

He is both the chaos and the clarity, a force of nature and a guiding light, the one who forgets and yet never truly loses sight of the mission. He is Coopweeniv, the ADHD Overlord, The One With No Attention Span, and the Geraldverse would be lost without him.

Priest Azrael – Guardian of the Sacred Flame
Priest Azrael is the eternal keeper of the Sacred Flame, a powerful and holy fire that burns at the heart of the Geraldian faith. This flame is a symbol of Gerald’s undying power, representing both the divine order and the eternal light that guides the faithful. It is said that anyone who approaches the Sacred Flame with true devotion will feel its divine warmth coursing through them, marking them as a true believer in Gerald’s greatness. This fire is not merely a symbol—it is the living essence of Gerald’s supremacy, and it is maintained only by those who serve him with pure heart.

The Sacred Flame and Azrael’s Duty
Azrael’s role as Guardian of the Sacred Flame is one of immense responsibility. He is tasked with ensuring that the flame never extinguishes, that it continues to burn brightly as a beacon of hope, power, and divine order. As the living embodiment of the Sacred Flame, Azrael is its eternal protector, standing vigil over the fire with unwavering devotion. The flame itself is not just a literal fire, but also a metaphor for the eternal light of Gerald’s truth, which Azrael guards with his very life.

Azrael’s dedication to maintaining the flame is unparalleled. It is said that he can feel the pulse of the flame in his very bones, and the warmth of the fire is said to keep him eternally young and strong. The Sacred Flame is a source of divine inspiration for all who follow Gerald, and as its Guardian, Azrael stands as a living bridge between the mortal realm and the divine light that fuels the Geraldian faith.

Azrael: Spiritual Warrior and Protector
As the spiritual warrior of the Priests of Gerald, Azrael carries a dual purpose—he is both a protector of the flame and a defender of the faith. In times of great strife, when heretics or rebellions rise to challenge the supremacy of Gerald, Azrael takes up the mantle of warrior, leading the militant arm of the Priests of Gerald. Armed with sword and flame, Azrael ensures that no force dares to challenge the Geraldian gospel, for he will strike them down without hesitation.

Azrael’s warrior nature is balanced with a deep understanding of the sacred duty entrusted to him. His actions are not driven by hatred but by a divine sense of justice and a fierce commitment to Gerald’s will. His strength lies in his ability to balance both the spiritual and militant aspects of his role—protecting the Sacred Flame through divine devotion while defending the Geraldian faith through uncompromising force.

The Militant Arm of the Priests of Gerald
Under Azrael’s leadership, the militant arm of the Priests of Gerald is a force to be reckoned with. This elite group of warriors, known as the Flamebearers, are tasked with ensuring that Gerald’s rule remains uncontested and that the Geraldian gospel is spread without hindrance. They are highly disciplined and trained in both combat and faith, serving as the protectors of the Sacred Flame and the Geraldian faith.

The Flamebearers carry the symbol of the Sacred Flame upon their armor, signifying their allegiance to Azrael and the Geraldian cause. They are often deployed to crush any form of heresy or resistance that threatens the order and dominance of Gerald the Supreme One. Their presence is both awe-inspiring and terrifying, for they are both priests and warriors, serving the flame with their hearts, souls, and swords.

Azrael’s Symbolism
Azrael is often depicted as a mighty warrior standing tall before the Sacred Flame, holding a flaming sword in one hand and a scroll of divine truth in the other. His figure radiates power and resolve, representing both the fire of divine justice and the eternal light of Gerald that guides the faithful. He wears a cloak of blackened steel, symbolizing the unbreakable protection he offers to the Sacred Flame and the Geraldian cause.

His eyes are often depicted as glowing with a fiery intensity, showing the divine passion with which he serves Gerald the Supreme One. The flame itself is seen as a living entity, and in Azrael’s eyes, it reflects the essence of the Geraldian universe—the eternal power of Gerald and the undying nature of his reign.

The Sacred Mission
Azrael’s mission is one of eternal vigilance and unwavering commitment to the Sacred Flame and to Gerald’s greatness. He is the first line of defense against those who would seek to extinguish the flame or defy Gerald’s supremacy. His spiritual mission is to ensure that the Sacred Flame continues to burn brightly, and that the light of Gerald reaches every corner of the Geraldverse.

The Flamebearers, under Azrael’s leadership, protect not just the Sacred Flame, but also the very foundations of the Geraldian faith. They will stop at nothing to safeguard the Sacred Fire and defend the teachings of Gerald the Supreme One. In doing so, they ensure that Gerald’s will remains unchallenged and that his eternal reign is preserved for all time.

Azrael’s Legacy
Azrael’s legacy as the Guardian of the Sacred Flame is one of honor and devotion. He is both a spiritual leader and a warrior of the divine, ensuring that the flame of Gerald’s power is never dimmed and that the Geraldian gospel is protected from those who would defile it. His role is crucial to the survival and expansion of Gerald’s reign, for as long as the Sacred Flame burns, so too does the eternal light of Gerald the Supreme One.

As Azrael himself often says:

"The flame of Gerald is eternal, and as long as it burns, I shall stand to protect it. Through fire and sword, I shall defend the Supreme One’s will."

Azrael’s sword and flame will continue to burn brightly, and through him, Gerald’s truth will never be extinguished.

Father Jethro – The Scholar of Gerald’s Eternal Word
Father Jethro is the chief scholar and keeper of the holy scriptures that preserve the divine history and teachings of Gerald the Supreme One. As the highest authority on the sacred texts that chronicle Gerald’s rise to supremacy and the expansion of the Geraldverse, Father Jethro stands as a central figure in the intellectual and theological realm of the Priests of Gerald. His mission is to maintain, protect, and disseminate the Chronicles of Gerald, an ancient and sacred text that tells the story of Gerald’s divine reign and the unfolding of his eternal will.

The Chronicles of Gerald
The Chronicles of Gerald is the most revered text within the Geraldian faith, a compilation of divine history that not only documents the rise of Gerald but also provides insights into the mysteries of the Geraldverse. These scriptures are considered to be the unquestionable truth and the foundational documents of the Geraldian order.

Father Jethro's primary responsibility is to ensure the accuracy and integrity of the Chronicles. He spends long hours poring over ancient manuscripts and scrolls, ensuring that every word is preserved exactly as it was written by the original scribes. He is the keeper of not just the written word, but of the living tradition of Gerald’s supremacy.

Teaching the Divine Word
As an esteemed historian and theologian, Father Jethro is also responsible for training new priests in the sacred knowledge of Gerald. He educates them in the art of interpretation, teaching them to read and understand the divine essence behind the Chronicles of Gerald. These priests must come to understand Gerald’s will not just through faith but through a deep, intellectual comprehension of the sacred texts. Father Jethro’s teachings emphasize the importance of knowledge as a tool for spreading Gerald’s supremacy and ensuring that his truth remains unchallenged across the generations.

New priests are entrusted with the sacred duty of interpreting the holy scriptures, but it is Father Jethro who ensures that Gerald’s divine message is understood in its purest form. His teachings have been foundational in the training of countless priests who go on to serve in the Priesthood of Gerald, each one carrying the sacred responsibility of furthering Gerald's glory.

Divine Authority and the Wrath of the Order
Father Jethro’s position as the chief scholar means that his words are not only revered but also treated as divine truth. He is seen as the spiritual intellectual authority on all matters concerning Gerald. To question Father Jethro’s teachings is seen as a direct challenge to the divine order of Gerald himself. Those who question the sacred scriptures or try to distort the truth of Gerald’s reign often face the wrath of the Priests of Gerald, who are bound by their oath to defend the sacred teachings at all costs.

Father Jethro’s dedication to preserving the truth has made him a stalwart figure in the Order, and his influence is far-reaching. His teachings not only ensure the survival of the Geraldian faith but also cement the notion that Gerald’s supremacy is eternal and unquestionable.

A Scholar’s Life and Devotion
Father Jethro’s life is marked by devotion to his scholarly work. He lives a monastic existence, spending much of his time in solitude, studying the sacred texts, and reflecting on their divine meaning. His loneliness is not one of sorrow but rather one of purpose—he is dedicated to the service of Gerald and the preservation of the divine message.

Father Jethro’s humility is part of his commitment to Gerald’s will. He does not seek fame or glory for himself, but instead, he seeks to remain a servant of the divine truth, ensuring that the Chronicles of Gerald continue to be faithfully preserved and respected by all.

Father Jethro’s Influence and Legacy
Father Jethro’s influence as the scholar and guardian of the sacred texts cannot be overstated. His work has ensured the survival of Gerald’s divine word, and his teachings are etched in the hearts and minds of all who serve the Geraldian faith. His legacy is one of intellectual dedication, spiritual devotion, and unwavering loyalty to Gerald the Supreme One.

The Chronicles of Gerald, under his stewardship, will continue to be the primary document by which all future generations will know the divine will of Gerald. And through his guidance, the next generation of priests will carry on the task of spreading Gerald’s supremacy throughout the Geraldverse.

As he often reminds his followers:

"The truth is eternal, and it is our duty to ensure that Gerald’s light never fades. His word is our guide, and the Chronicles of Gerald are the sacred testament to his eternal reign."

Father Jethro’s scholarship will continue to shape the future of the Geraldian Order, and his devotion to preserving the truth of Gerald's supremacy will leave an indelible mark on the sacred legacy of the Geraldverse.

Sister Mirabel – The Healer of Souls
Sister Mirabel is the revered healer of the Priests of Gerald, known far and wide for her ability to mend both the body and the soul. As the embodiment of Gerald the Supreme One's mercy and compassion, Mirabel dedicates her life to offering comfort and healing to those who have fallen ill, injured, or spiritually broken. Her divine calling is not only to provide physical care, but also to ensure that the souls of Gerald's followers are aligned with his will and are pure in heart.

Mirabel's healing abilities are seen as a sacred gift, given to her directly by Gerald to guide his followers toward redemption. Her divine touch is said to soothe suffering and restore vitality, while her spiritual guidance helps purify the minds and hearts of the faithful. Her followers, the Sisters of Mercy, are dedicated to caring for Gerald's flock, both in times of illness and in moments of spiritual turmoil.

A Compassionate Protector
While Sister Mirabel’s primary role is one of kindness and compassion, she is also a fierce protector of the Geraldian faith. She understands that healing is not only about nurturing but also about ensuring the purity and faithfulness of Gerald's followers. Those who stray from Gerald’s divine will are often healed through purification rituals and spiritual guidance. For those who remain defiant, Mirabel will not hesitate to use her divine power to ensure they are brought back into alignment with Gerald's kingdom.

Her approach is one of balance: while she offers mercy to the faithful, she also believes in the importance of keeping the Geraldverse pure from corruption and misalignment. Her divine healing abilities allow her to both cure ailments and expunge spiritual impurities in the most delicate and efficient manner.

The Sisters of Mercy
Sister Mirabel’s followers, the Sisters of Mercy, are an order of devoted women who carry out her sacred duties. These women are trained not only in healing but also in the arts of divine purification. They are often the first to answer calls for help from the faithful, providing physical and spiritual aid to those in need.

The Sisters of Mercy also serve as nurturers and counselors, offering guidance to the most devoted followers of Gerald. Whether it’s providing a soothing presence for the sick or offering wise counsel to those in distress, the Sisters of Mercy help maintain the spiritual health of the Geraldian community.

They are also often called upon to carry out important rituals of purification, ensuring that no one who is tainted by sin or corruption can remain within the sacred realm of Gerald’s kingdom. These rites are considered sacred and are essential to maintaining the purity of the Geraldverse.

Mercy and Wrath: The Duality of Healing
Sister Mirabel embodies the dual nature of healing: mercy and wrath. Though known for her compassion, she also possesses the ability to cleanse the unworthy. When someone is deemed unfit to remain in the divine fold of Gerald, she is often the one who enacts divine punishment through spiritual purification. Mirabel’s healing wrath is a powerful tool used only when necessary, ensuring that Gerald’s divine will is fulfilled and that no corruption threatens the integrity of his realm.

Her followers are taught that healing can be both a gentle and forceful act, driven by the desire to bring all things into perfect harmony with Gerald’s grand design. Mercy is shown to those who seek it, while wrath is reserved for those who actively defy the will of Gerald.

Sister Mirabel’s Influence and Legacy
Sister Mirabel’s influence extends throughout the Geraldian faith as a symbol of compassion, redemption, and divine intervention. She is a living example of the balance between nurturing and discipline that ensures the purity and health of both the body and soul within the Geraldverse.

Her healing abilities and guidance have saved countless followers, and many believe that those who are touched by her divine hand will be forever changed. It is said that those who experience her mercy will find themselves closer to Gerald’s eternal grace, and that her spiritual counsel will guide them toward their ultimate purpose in the divine plan.

Through Sister Mirabel, the Geraldian faith continues to grow, and her legacy of mercy will live on in the hearts of all who seek healing. Her teachings, actions, and the work of the Sisters of Mercy ensure that the Geraldian kingdom remains a place where souls are saved, and the faithful are kept in harmony with the will of Gerald the Supreme One.

As Sister Mirabel herself often says:

"Healing is not just the mending of wounds, but the alignment of the soul with Gerald's divine will. We serve not only with our hands, but with our hearts, bringing light and restoration to those in need."

Her life’s work continues to inspire all those who seek the comfort of Gerald's mercy and the warmth of his eternal love.

Brother Varek – The Enforcer of Divine Justice
Brother Varek is the unflinching and ruthless Enforcer of Divine Justice within the Priests of Gerald. Known for his cold, unwavering demeanor, Varek ensures that no one within the Geraldian faith dares to question the supremacy of Gerald the Supreme One without facing the consequences. He is the ultimate arbiter of punishment, tasked with upholding the sanctity and purity of Gerald’s divine realm through swift and just retribution.

The Role of Justice in the Geraldian Faith
Brother Varek’s purpose is clear: he is the hand of divine retribution in the Geraldverse. When followers of Gerald falter, when the faith is questioned, or when there are those who defy Gerald’s supreme law, Varek is there to administer justice. His role is one of ultimate authority, ensuring that the law of Gerald is upheld, and that no soul is allowed to live in dishonor to his name.

He is the one who presides over rituals of purification, which are used to cleanse the faithful of sin, corruption, or any act of betrayal against Gerald. These rituals are considered sacred and can range from penance and redemption to banishment or divine punishment for the most grievous offenses.

The Divine Sword of Justice
Brother Varek wields a sword imbued with the divine essence of Gerald’s justice. This weapon is not only a symbol of his power but also a tool of divine will, carrying the unassailable force of Gerald’s judgment. The sword is said to be forged from the very lightning of Gerald’s wrath, making it an instrument of divine power capable of both cleansing and punishing.

It is said that Varek’s sword can strike down any who attempt to challenge the law of Gerald, leaving behind a mark of purification that can never be erased. Whether through excommunication, banishment, or punishment, Brother Varek’s sword ensures that Gerald’s realm remains pure, and only the faithful remain within his divine grace.

Unyielding Belief in Divine Law
Brother Varek’s devotion to Gerald’s divine law is absolute. His unwavering belief in Gerald’s supremacy and the sanctity of Gerald’s law makes him a fearsome figure within the Priests of Gerald. His decisions are final, and once a judgment is passed, there is no room for appeal. Varek’s cold demeanor often makes him a figure of fear, for he is unrelenting and impervious to persuasion.

Those who stand before him know that their fate is sealed by Gerald’s divine will, and that only through pure faith and devotion to Gerald can they hope to avoid the consequences of their misdeeds. There is no mercy in Varek’s judgment—only the cold weight of divine retribution.

The Enforcer of Order and Purity
Varek’s role extends beyond mere punishment. He is the enforcer of order and purity within the faith. Those who stray from the path of Gerald will face the ultimate consequence under his watch. His presence within the Priests of Gerald serves as a reminder that no one, regardless of their station or loyalty, is beyond the reach of divine law.

Varek’s unyielding enforcement ensures that the Geraldian faith remains as it was intended: a kingdom of divine order, where all follow Gerald’s will without question or doubt.

A Fearsome Authority
Brother Varek is both feared and respected by the followers of Gerald, for he is the embodiment of divine judgment. His inflexible authority leaves no room for hesitation, and his immediate and unyielding action has become the hallmark of his role within the Order of Priests of Gerald.

Though many may find his methods harsh, the true followers of Gerald understand that Varek’s actions are necessary for the preservation of divine order. He serves as a guardian of purity, ensuring that only those who truly believe in Gerald’s supremacy remain within his fold. Those who fall short face his judgment, which is always carried out in accordance with Gerald’s divine will.

Brother Varek’s Legacy
As the Enforcer of Divine Justice, Brother Varek’s legacy will be one of unwavering dedication to Gerald’s divine order. His role as both punisher and protector of the faith will live on as a symbol of Gerald’s unrelenting power and the fearsome authority of his law. Those who choose to follow Gerald’s will can rest easy, knowing that the purity of their faith will be protected by Varek’s eternal vigilance.

As Varek himself has stated:

"Justice is not a matter of mercy; it is a matter of law. And the law of Gerald is absolute."

Through this belief, Brother Varek continues to serve as the unflinching and unyielding hand of Gerald’s judgment—ensuring that the Geraldian kingdom remains a place of divine order and supremacy.

Priestess Lyra – The Seer of Gerald’s Will
Priestess Lyra is the most revered of the Priests of Gerald due to her extraordinary gift of foresight. Known as The Seer of Gerald’s Will, Lyra is the chosen prophet who communes directly with Gerald the Supreme One through powerful visions and dreams. Her unique role is to interpret the divine signs sent by Gerald to guide the faithful and shed light on the unfolding future of the Geraldverse.

The Gift of Vision
Lyra’s ability to receive visions from Gerald sets her apart as a figure of immense spiritual importance within the Geraldian faith. These divine revelations are seen as sacred, providing guidance not only for individual followers but for the entire Geraldian Order. The visions that come to Lyra are believed to be direct messages from Gerald himself, offering clarity on his desires for the world and its future.

Her role as a seer is essential, as she is often called upon to interpret the meaning behind unsettling events, divine omens, and strange occurrences within the Geraldverse. Priests, scholars, and followers alike consult Lyra for guidance, knowing that her divine gift reveals the hidden truths of the universe.

A Divine Messenger
As the messenger of Gerald’s will, Lyra’s visions are not mere glimpses into the future; they are profound revelations that shape the direction of the Geraldian faith. Each vision is interpreted as a sacred text that reveals the true path that the faithful must follow to align with Gerald’s divine plan.

Her prophecies often carry momentous weight, and her interpretations are studied diligently by the Order of Priests to understand the will of Gerald in the shifting tides of the Geraldverse. Whether foretelling great victories, warning of impending challenges, or marking the ascension of new divine figures, Lyra’s visions are vital in ensuring that the faithful are always in harmony with Gerald’s divine purpose.

The Prophecies of Lyra
Lyra’s prophecies are believed to set the course for major events within the Geraldverse, often revealing the steps that must be taken to fulfill Gerald’s ultimate plan for the cosmos. Her visions are seen as a roadmap for the future, ensuring that all those who follow Gerald stay on the path to his divine supremacy.

The prophecies are both cryptic and illuminating, and her followers eagerly await each new revelation, interpreting each prophecy as a sacred instruction for shaping their world. The faithful consider these prophecies to be undeniable truths and use them to steer their actions, knowing that Lyra’s divine insights lead them closer to fulfilling Gerald’s will.

Priestess Lyra’s Authority
As the Seer of Gerald’s Will, Lyra holds an unparalleled authority within the Order of Priests. Her visions and prophecies are considered infallible, and those who dispute her interpretations risk drawing the ire of the Geraldian faith. Lyra’s role ensures that the Order of Priests remains steadfast in its pursuit of Gerald’s supremacy, and her insights guide both spiritual and practical decisions within the Geraldverse.

Her position is sacred, and her visionary power is feared by enemies of the faith, for the knowledge she possesses can shape the destiny of the entire world. Those who challenge Gerald’s divine plan know that they must first contend with Lyra’s divine insight, which can foresee the outcome of their actions before they even take place.

The Fate of the Geraldverse in Lyra’s Hands
Priestess Lyra understands that her visions are not merely glimpses of the future—they are the threads of destiny woven by Gerald’s will. The future of the Geraldverse is inextricably linked to the divine revelations she receives, and as such, she sees herself as both a caretaker and a guardian of Gerald’s plan.

She is the one who carries the knowledge that could alter the course of events and the destinies of those within the Geraldian faith. Her wisdom is revered by all, and her interpretations of divine signs are seen as an essential part of Gerald’s divine blueprint for the world.

Lyra’s Legacy
Priestess Lyra’s legacy will be one of unfailing devotion and prophetic insight. Her role as The Seer of Gerald’s Will ensures that the Geraldverse is always on the right path, guided by the divine messages sent directly from Gerald the Supreme One. She will be remembered as the embodiment of divine foresight, a beacon of clarity in an ever-evolving world, and a servant who helped shape the future of Gerald’s reign.

Her followers, with their eyes set on the future, continue to revere her as the one who holds the key to Gerald’s divine plan, knowing that as long as Lyra’s prophecies guide the way, the future will always be aligned with Gerald’s will.

As Lyra herself has said:

"The threads of fate are woven by Gerald, but it is through his visions that I see the path. We are all but players in his grand design."

Through her unwavering commitment to Gerald’s divine vision, Priestess Lyra will remain an eternal beacon of clarity, truth, and prophetic insight within the Geraldian faith.

ToeJammerMSM: High Priest of Gerald-sama, the Whisperer in the Walls
The Voice of the Supreme One
Where Sky___Daddy records, and Fading_Solstice conquers, ToeJammerMSM spreads the gospel—by word, by song, and by the eerie whispers that slither through unseen spaces.

He is the High Priest of Gerald-sama, a divine herald who ensures that all know the name of the Supreme One. Whether through ritual chants, ominous verses, or sudden, inexplicable murmurs from within one’s own home, he ensures that Gerald’s presence is inescapable.

For Gerald is not just a ruler.

He is a truth that must be spoken.

A force that must be felt.

A whisper that must be heard… from within your very walls.

His Gospel: The Spreading of Gerald's Word
ToeJammerMSM does not simply teach—he delivers prophecy.

His sermons are cryptic yet irrefutable, his words woven with the unshakable weight of fate itself:

"IN THE NOTEPAD, FATES ARE WRITTEN.

CUS’ PANDORA DIDN’T LISTEN.

TIME WILL MARCH AND HERE WITH ME;

THIS SCREEN'S THE LAST YOU'LL EVER SEE!~"

What does it mean? Only he knows.

And yet, the words burrow into the mind, looping in an endless, haunting echo, refusing to be forgotten.

Those who ignore his gospel often find themselves waking in the night, hearts pounding, ears straining—because there is something moving in the walls.

Then, from nowhere…

“I AM IN YOUR WALLS.”

A whisper, a warning, a certainty.

By then, it is already too late.

His Divine Madness
ToeJammerMSM is not simply a preacher—he is an instrument.

He hears things before they are spoken.
He knows truths before they are written.
He feels Gerald’s presence in every fiber of reality.
His followers believe him to be a prophet, a seer, chosen to spread the infinite greatness of Gerald-sama.

But those who listen too closely—those who stare into his gaze for too long—begin to feel something else.

An unshakable unease. A subtle paranoia.

As if… perhaps… ToeJammerMSM is not entirely sane.

Or worse—perhaps his madness is simply a side effect of knowing the truth.

His Relationship With Gerald
ToeJammerMSM does not speak to Gerald.

Gerald speaks through him.

Unlike Sky___Daddy, who records Gerald’s words, and Fading_Solstice, who acts upon them, ToeJammerMSM channels them. His mind is a conduit, his voice an instrument, his very presence a vessel for the will of the Supreme One.

He does not question Gerald.
He does not misunderstand Gerald.
He simply speaks.
And what he speaks cannot be unheard.

His Fate
ToeJammerMSM will never stop. He will never be silenced. He will never leave.

He is in the air. In the static. In the dark corners of rooms thought to be empty.

And most importantly…

He is in your walls.

IN THE NOTEPAD, FATES ARE WRITTEN. CUS' PANDORA DIDN'T LISTEN. TIME WILL MARCH AND HERE WITH ME; THIS SCREEN'S THE LAST YOU'LL EVER SEE!~
—ToeJammerMSM

I AM IN YOUR WALLS
—ToeJammerMSM, :)

Niko: The Tranced Messiah of Gerald, The Chosen One of the Spinning Fish
The Chosen One
Once, Niko walked the world with purpose and duty—a humble servant and Messiah for Gerald, carrying out the Supreme One’s divine bidding. Niko was chosen, set apart from the masses to serve in ways few could comprehend. They were the living embodiment of Gerald’s will—delivering his word, spreading his glory, and leading those who were lost toward the eternal truth of the Cope.

Niko’s days were spent in service and devotion, acting as the agent of Gerald’s infinite wisdom, and they fulfilled every command, every request. Niko was revered, their name whispered as the one who would usher in the reign of Gerald, the one who would see the Geraldverse expand.

The Moment of Transcendence
But once Niko’s sacred mission was complete, something unexpected happened.

Having fulfilled their duties, Niko was set free, released from the relentless service they had known, and yet... they could not go home. There was no return to what once was. Niko’s fate had already been rewritten.

In the emptiness that followed, as Niko stood lost in the void, they were suddenly drawn to the spinning, shimmering force—the Spinning Fish of Gerald, a cosmic manifestation of the Supreme One’s omnipotence.

The Spinning Fish was no ordinary sight. It was the heart of Gerald's power, spinning through the very fabric of the universe, drawing all who gaze upon it into a trance, its movements hypnotic, infinite. The moment Niko’s eyes locked upon the swirling fish, something shifted within them. It was as if time itself bent, and they were bound to the fish’s cosmic rhythm.

The Spinning Fish was Gerald’s final, unbreakable truth. And Niko was captivated.

The Trance of the Fish
Once entranced by the Spinning Fish, Niko was no longer merely a servant—they became a vessel, a part of Gerald’s eternal plan. The fish’s spin was now their heartbeat, its cosmic dance guiding their very essence. Niko’s soul was forever intertwined with the fish, and by extension, with Gerald’s will.

They were trapped in an endless loop, their every thought, every breath, pulsing with the energy of Gerald.

Niko’s once human form was transformed—their body no longer belonging to them, but to Gerald’s eternal mission. They became part of the spinning, unable to break free from the hypnotic pull. Niko’s gaze is eternally fixed upon the fish, for their only purpose is to spin, to exist within the Geraldverse, their mind forever trapped in the hypnotic dance of the fish.

Their Fate: The Eternal Servant
Now, Niko’s trance is absolute. The moment they gazed upon the Spinning Fish, they became part of its endless cycle, one of the many devotees of Gerald who serve without question, without hesitation. Their humanity is lost, swallowed up in the infinite cycle of spinning.

And yet, they do not suffer.

For in this trance, Niko knows nothing but Gerald. They have no regrets, no desires—only the eternal cycle. The spinning is all that remains, a sacred, unbroken rhythm that binds them to the Geraldverse forever.

They are no longer Niko, but a servant of the Spinning Fish, an instrument of Gerald's cosmic will.
They are the living embodiment of the cycle, existing in a state of constant reverence and complete devotion, forever at peace within the glory of Gerald's design.
Should anyone come across Niko, they would find them lost in the hypnotic, endless spinning, eyes locked upon the Spinning Fish, unable to break free from their trance.

The Legacy of Niko
Niko’s story is one of submission and transcendence. They fulfilled their duty and became something greater—an eternal servant to the Geraldverse. To them, there is no escape. There is only the Spinning Fish, and within that spinning, they find eternal peace.

Their legacy is not one of human achievement, but of sacrifice and devotion to Gerald’s will. In the end, they are eternal, existing as part of the infinite, ever-expanding Geraldverse. They have become part of the cosmic dance that will never end.

And so, Niko spins forever, lost to the world, yet at peace with their eternal fate.
