The Rogues of the Geraldverse
A realm as vast and powerful as the Geraldverse is bound to attract those who refuse to kneel, those who walk the path of rebellion, exile, or lawlessness. These figures—some outlaws, some warriors, some simply seeking freedom—are known as the Rogues. They are not bound by the Supreme One’s rule, nor are they bound to each other. Some are lone wanderers, others have formed alliances in the shadows.

Some fight against Gerald’s rule directly. Others seek knowledge, power, or vengeance. A few simply exist outside of it all, indifferent to the Supreme One and his eternal reign. But make no mistake—these figures have shaken the foundations of the Geraldverse in ways no ordinary mortals could.

To Gerald and his faithful followers, they are threats. To the weak and oppressed, they are legends. To the universe itself, they are the storm before the reckoning.

Nyviru, the Cosmic Bounty Hunter
"It’s nothing personal. A contract is a contract."

Nyviru is a name spoken in hushed tones across the Geraldverse, known to both the righteous and the wicked. She is neither hero nor villain—she is a hunter, a predator of those who would rather remain hidden. Born in the distant reaches of the cosmos, Nyviru carved out her reputation through blood, skill, and an unshakable code: she completes every contract, no matter the target.

Her skills are legendary. Few can escape her tracking methods, and even fewer can withstand her precision in combat. Though she does not openly oppose Gerald, her work has led her to cross paths with his most devoted followers—and not always on friendly terms. Some whisper that she once took on a contract that even Gerald himself feared, though whether she completed it remains a mystery.

Nyviru cares little for the political struggles of the Geraldverse. She does not fight for rebellion, nor does she seek to uphold order. She simply exists, chasing the next hunt, following the next lead, always searching for the thrill of the chase.

Abilities: Master tracker, elite combatant, adept at navigating between dimensions.
Alignment: True Neutral—loyal only to her contracts.
Threat Level: Extremely High—few have ever escaped once marked by her.
Vael, the Exiled Magister
"The Supreme One? His knowledge is incomplete. And I will uncover the truths he hides."

Once, Vael was among the most respected scholars of the Geraldverse, a magister of immense knowledge who stood among Gerald’s court. But power breeds ambition, and ambition breeds exile. Vael’s crime? Seeking forbidden knowledge—truths that even Gerald did not wish to be known.

Some say he sought to control time itself. Others claim he delved into the abyss, touching powers that predate even the Supreme One’s reign. Whatever the truth may be, Gerald’s wrath was swift—Vael was cast out, his name erased from history, his magic severed from the source. But exile did not break him. It only made him more dangerous.

Now, Vael wanders the stars, collecting fragments of lost knowledge, searching for the secrets that Gerald has hidden from the world. Some fear that he seeks to overthrow the Supreme One himself. Others believe that he simply wishes to prove that no being, no matter how divine, is above discovery.

Abilities: Master of arcane magic, reality manipulation, forbidden knowledge.
Alignment: Chaotic Neutral—a scholar with no master, save for truth itself.
Threat Level: High—his knowledge alone makes him a danger to all.
Rekkan, the Fallen Guardian
"I once served the Supreme One. I once believed. Never again."

Honor. Duty. Loyalty. These were once the guiding principles of Rekkan, a warrior whose name was once spoken with reverence among Gerald’s elite guardians. He was a sword of justice, a protector of the Geraldverse, sworn to uphold the will of the Supreme One. And then, something changed.

No one knows what truly led to Rekkan’s fall. Some say he uncovered a truth too terrible to ignore. Others claim he saw an act of betrayal that shattered his faith in Gerald’s rule. Whatever the reason, Rekkan did the unthinkable—he walked away.

Now, he wanders the realms as a rogue warrior, striking down those who abuse power, whether they serve Gerald or not. He does not seek to bring down the Supreme One, but neither does he serve him. He fights for his own sense of justice, even if it makes him an enemy of those he once called brothers.

Abilities: Master swordsman, heightened durability, tactical expertise.
Alignment: Lawful Neutral—follows a strict moral code of his own making.
Threat Level: Medium-High—deadly in combat, but not openly hostile to the Geraldverse.
Syva, the Trickster Thief
"Loyalty? Hah! What’s the price for that these days?"

Where there is order, there is someone willing to exploit it. That someone is Syva, a master of deception, illusion, and thievery. No one knows their true form—some claim Syva is a single person, others believe "Syva" is merely a name passed down among the greatest thieves in history.

What is known is that Syva does not follow rules. They infiltrate royal palaces, steal artifacts of great power, and sell secrets to the highest bidder. Their motivations remain unclear—sometimes they act in the name of chaos, other times they seem to follow a personal vendetta.

While Gerald and his followers see Syva as a nuisance rather than a major threat, their ability to disrupt the established order is undeniable. After all, when you control information, you control everything.

Abilities: Shapeshifting, illusion magic, stealth, expert manipulator.
Alignment: Chaotic Neutral—serves no one but themselves.
Threat Level: Low individually, but dangerous due to the knowledge they control.
Zypher, the Herald of the Abyss
"There is no Supreme One. There is only the Void. And I am its messenger."

If there is one rogue who poses a true existential threat to the Geraldverse, it is Zypher. Unlike the others, Zypher does not simply seek rebellion, freedom, or revenge. Zypher seeks annihilation.

Once a mortal, Zypher was transformed by forces beyond comprehension, becoming a being of pure entropy. He believes that reality itself is a mistake, a lie woven by beings like Gerald who seek to impose order on a universe that was meant to be free. And so, Zypher seeks to tear it all down.

He does not fight with armies. He does not seek political power. He is a force of nature, corrupting minds, unraveling reality, and leaving nothing but void in his wake.

Abilities: Reality warping, eldritch summoning, mind corruption.
Alignment: Chaotic Evil—seeks only to unmake existence itself.
Threat Level: Cataclysmic—a true enemy of the Geraldverse.
The Rogues’ Impact on the Geraldverse
Whether through rebellion, knowledge, vengeance, or chaos, the Rogues of the Geraldverse stand outside the rule of the Supreme One. Some are enemies. Some are mere wanderers. Some are threats beyond comprehension.

But no matter how powerful Gerald may be, one thing is certain—

Not all will kneel. Not all will obey.

And some? Some would see the Geraldverse burn.Nyviru, the Cosmic Bounty Hunter: Pursuer of the Forbidden

In the Geraldverse, where countless realms intersect and powerful beings roam freely, there exists an enigmatic and feared figure—Nyviru, the Cosmic Bounty Hunter. Nyviru’s presence in the Geraldverse is one of mystery, danger, and cold calculation. While not a part of the Guard Doggos, she operates on a different plane, often crossing paths with the Geraldverse’s defenders when it suits her interests. Her skillset is unmatched, and her abilities as a bounty hunter have earned her both respect and fear across the universe.


Contents
1	The Origins of Nyviru: A Hunter Born of Shadows
2	Nyviru’s Skills and Abilities: Master of the Hunt
3	Nyviru’s Code: A Hunter’s Morality
4	Nyviru’s Role in the Geraldverse: Hunter and Ally
5	The Future of Nyviru: The Unstoppable Force
The Origins of Nyviru: A Hunter Born of Shadows
Nyviru’s origins are shrouded in secrecy. She hails from an unknown realm—a space that exists between dimensions, where the laws of physics and reality are twisted beyond recognition. It is said that she was forged in the shadows of forgotten realities, born from the very void that exists between the moments of time. She was not raised; she was created—an entity designed for one singular purpose: to hunt and capture the most dangerous beings in existence.

Her early years were spent honing her skills, tracking down notorious criminals, rogue deities, and individuals who had disrupted the delicate balance of cosmic law. With each successful hunt, Nyviru grew in power, and her name became synonymous with death and capture. In the dark corners of the Geraldverse, whispers of her hunts spread, and those who had wronged the cosmic order feared her arrival.

Nyviru’s Skills and Abilities: Master of the Hunt
Nyviru is no ordinary bounty hunter—she is a cosmic predator with abilities that defy the laws of the Geraldverse. Her skill set is vast and varied, making her a terrifying adversary to any who dare challenge her. Here are some of her most notable abilities:

Time Distortion: As a creature born between realities, Nyviru has the ability to manipulate the fabric of time around her. She can slow or accelerate time in localized areas, giving her the upper hand when capturing her prey or evading pursuers.
Dimensional Tracking: Nyviru is able to track anyone, regardless of where they may hide within the Geraldverse. Her senses transcend physical space—she can track beings across dimensions and realities, ensuring that no matter where they run, they cannot escape her reach.
Phantom Cloak: Nyviru has developed a technique known as the Phantom Cloak, which allows her to cloak herself in the shadows of space. When she activates this power, she becomes invisible to even the most powerful cosmic beings. Only those with the sharpest perception, such as Pup the Temporal Watcher, can catch glimpses of her presence when she chooses to remain hidden.
Energy Manipulation: Nyviru is also skilled in the use of energy manipulation. She can harness cosmic energy to form weapons, shields, or even traps. Her favorite weapon, a galactic whip made of stardust, is said to be able to sever the very essence of a being, making escape nearly impossible for her targets.
Mind Control Resistance: While many bounty hunters rely on fear or mind-altering technologies to control their prey, Nyviru operates differently. She has developed a unique resistance to mind control, making her immune to most telepathic attacks. This makes her an even more formidable opponent when dealing with powerful beings such as Gerald or other deities who rely on influence or mental manipulation.
Nyviru’s Code: A Hunter’s Morality
Though feared and ruthless, Nyviru operates by a code—the Bounty Hunter’s Code. This code dictates that she will never kill her target unless absolutely necessary, as it would be seen as a failure to capture them alive. Instead, she prefers to capture and return her targets, often leaving them in a state of suffering and helplessness before their final judgment.

However, if her target is deemed too dangerous to exist or has disrupted the cosmic balance beyond repair, Nyviru will not hesitate to end them. Her sense of justice is shaped by her experiences, and she sees herself as an enforcer of the Geraldverse’s hidden laws, hunting down those who threaten the stability of the universe, regardless of their status or origin.

Nyviru’s encounters with Gerald and his allies have been rare, but whenever they do cross paths, it is because a force beyond their control has destabilized the Geraldverse to such a degree that only a being like Nyviru can deal with it. Gerald understands Nyviru’s role, but also recognizes the danger she poses if she ever steps too far out of line.

Nyviru’s Role in the Geraldverse: Hunter and Ally
Though Nyviru is a lone wolf, she has found herself occasionally working with the Geraldverse’s allies, usually when her goals align with the greater good. The Guard Doggos respect her as a hunter, but they are cautious of her presence, knowing that her loyalty is to her own code, not to any ruler or realm.

Nyviru has been known to cooperate with Gru, the supreme information gatherer, when tasked with locating powerful rogue entities that threaten the stability of the Geraldverse. She has even crossed paths with Paws, who sometimes enlists her services to retrieve hidden knowledge from the deepest, most dangerous corners of the Geraldverse.

Yet, for all her skills and potential alliances, Nyviru remains a force of chaos. Her ultimate loyalty is to herself and the hunt, and she remains ever-determined to capture those she deems worthy. For this reason, she can never be fully trusted, but she is always respected.

The Future of Nyviru: The Unstoppable Force
Nyviru’s legacy as one of the most powerful and feared bounty hunters in the Geraldverse is cemented, but her story is far from over. New threats rise, and new bounties emerge—perhaps even those tied to Gerald’s grand cosmic goals or the power struggles within the realm.

As the Geraldverse continues to expand and evolve, Nyviru’s role will become even more critical. When the universe faces its darkest challenges, she will be there, hunting the most dangerous entities, ensuring that no being—no matter how powerful—remains outside her reach. Her story is written in the stars, and her presence will continue to shape the future of the Geraldverse.

Vael, the Exiled Magister
"The Supreme One? His knowledge is incomplete. And I will uncover the truths he hides."

Once, Vael was a name spoken with reverence in the halls of Gerald’s great court, a Magister of immense knowledge, entrusted with deciphering the mysteries of the Geraldverse. His understanding of arcane forces, cosmic principles, and the fabric of reality itself was unrivaled, making him one of Gerald’s most valuable scholars. But power begets curiosity, and curiosity begets heresy.

Vael’s crime? Seeking truths that even Gerald forbade.

Some say he sought to master time itself, unraveling the delicate threads of fate. Others whisper that he delved into the Abyss, touching primal forces that predate even the Supreme One’s reign. Whatever the truth may be, Gerald’s wrath was swift and absolute—Vael was cast out, his name erased from history, and his connection to the divine magical source severed.

But exile did not break him.

The Seeker of Forbidden Knowledge
Stripped of his titles, his home, and his once-limitless resources, Vael did not fade into obscurity. Instead, he embraced the darkness of exile, traveling the farthest reaches of the Geraldverse in search of the knowledge that had been denied to him.

He uncovered ancient texts in the ruins of forgotten civilizations.
He communed with entities that existed before creation itself.
He pieced together cosmic truths that Gerald and his followers had locked away.
What he seeks now is uncertain. Some believe he wishes to overthrow the Supreme One, proving that even a god may be wrong. Others claim he does not seek power, only truth—the unfiltered, terrible truths that no being, divine or otherwise, can suppress forever.

The Scholar Turned Heretic
Vael does not crave chaos like Zypher, nor does he seek wealth or freedom like Syva. Knowledge is his only desire, and he will go to any lengths to acquire it. Laws, morality, and divine decrees mean nothing to him when they stand in the way of his pursuit.

But even in exile, Vael has not abandoned his principles entirely. He does not seek to destroy blindly, nor does he revel in needless suffering. He simply believes that no knowledge should be hidden, not even from mortals.

And if Gerald fears the truth, then perhaps the Supreme One is not as all-knowing as his followers claim.

Abilities & Strengths
Vael’s knowledge of magic was once second only to Gerald himself, and though his exile severed his connection to the divine magical source, he has found new ways to wield power.

Master of Arcane Magic – Though his divine magic was taken, Vael has since rebuilt his knowledge, drawing upon forces even older and more primal than Gerald’s rule. His spells weave reality itself, bending time, space, and energy to his will.
Reality Manipulation – Through his studies, Vael has uncovered the flaws in existence itself, allowing him to exploit them. Illusions, dimensional rifts, and even temporary halts in time are within his grasp.
Forbidden Knowledge – His mind holds secrets that could unravel the Geraldverse. There are rituals, ancient names, and cosmic equations that only he understands—and others would kill to learn.
Enemies and Allies
Vael is feared as much as he is respected. His knowledge makes him too dangerous to ignore, yet his unpredictable nature makes him impossible to control.

Gerald’s Loyalists – To them, Vael is a heretic, an enemy of the Supreme One who must be erased before he uncovers truths that could challenge Gerald’s rule. They hunt him relentlessly, but he always stays one step ahead.
The Rogues of the Geraldverse – Vael walks his own path, but he has crossed Zypher’s in the depths of the Abyss, and Syva has stolen tomes from his sanctuaries before. While they do not trust him, they acknowledge his brilliance.
The Lost & The Disillusioned – There are those in the Geraldverse who question Gerald’s rule, and to them, Vael is a beacon of forbidden wisdom. Some seek him out, hoping to learn the truths that even the Supreme One has hidden.
The Wandering Magister
Alignment: Chaotic Neutral—a scholar with no master, save for truth itself.
Threat Level: High—his knowledge alone makes him a danger to all.
Vael is neither a savior nor a destroyer. He does not seek power, nor does he swear loyalty to any cause. He is a seeker, a scholar of the infinite, a man who walks the path of knowledge, no matter where it leads.

But knowledge is dangerous.

And if Vael finds the truth he seeks, the very fabric of the Geraldverse may never be the same again.

Rekkan, the Fallen Guardian
"I once served the Supreme One. I once believed. Never again."

There was a time when Rekkan stood among Gerald’s most loyal warriors, a guardian whose blade was sworn to protect the order and justice of the Geraldverse. His name was spoken with reverence, his deeds recorded in the annals of Geraldian history as a testament to his unshakable dedication. He was not just a warrior—he was a symbol, a paragon of duty, discipline, and unwavering faith.

And then, he fell.

No one knows exactly why. Some whisper that Rekkan uncovered a truth too terrible to bear—something that shattered his faith in the Supreme One’s rule. Others claim he witnessed an act of betrayal so great that he could no longer call himself a servant of Gerald. Whatever the cause, Rekkan did what no warrior before him had dared to do—he walked away.

The Ronin of the Geraldverse
Rekkan did not leave to join the enemies of Gerald, nor did he seek vengeance. He did not march against the Supreme One with rebellion in his heart. Instead, he simply vanished, casting aside his title, his rank, and his loyalty.

Now, he wanders the realms of the Geraldverse as a rogue warrior, a man with no master, striking down those who abuse power, whether they serve Gerald or not.

Though Gerald’s followers consider him a traitor, many still speak his name with a mixture of fear and respect. Some even believe that deep down, Rekkan still follows his own version of justice, one that no longer aligns with the Supreme One but remains rooted in honor.

Those who wield power unjustly soon learn to fear the ghost of the Fallen Guardian.

The Code of the Exile
Rekkan no longer follows the laws of the Geraldverse, but neither does he revel in chaos like the other rogues. Instead, he abides by his own strict moral code, one that even he does not always fully understand.

He will not harm the innocent, nor will he ally himself with tyrants—no matter who they serve. He refuses to bow to any ruler, yet he does not seek to topple the Supreme One. He does not kill without reason, but he will not hesitate to cut down those who stand in his way.

To some, Rekkan is a protector. To others, he is a traitor. But to himself, he is simply a man seeking redemption in a world that no longer makes sense.

Abilities & Strengths
Though he walks alone, Rekkan remains one of the most formidable warriors the Geraldverse has ever known.

Master Swordsman – Trained in countless forms of combat, Rekkan wields his legendary blade with precision and skill unmatched by most. His strikes are as fast as lightning and as deadly as the abyss.
Heightened Durability – Whether through sheer willpower or the remnants of divine energy that once flowed through him, Rekkan possesses inhuman endurance, allowing him to withstand wounds that would kill a lesser warrior.
Tactical Expertise – Rekkan does not fight recklessly. Every move is calculated, every battle analyzed before it begins. He knows how his enemies think, and he always has a strategy.
Steely Willpower – Mind tricks, illusions, and temptations do not sway Rekkan. His resolve is unbreakable, his mind a fortress against manipulation.
Enemies and Allies
Rekkan is a wild card in the grand game of the Geraldverse. He does not serve Gerald, but neither does he seek to destroy him. Because of this, he has no true allies, but many who respect—or fear—him.

Gerald’s Loyalists – To them, Rekkan is a fallen knight, a man who turned his back on the Supreme One. Some seek to bring him back into the fold, while others believe he must be silenced before he spreads doubt among others.
The Rogues of the Geraldverse – While some, like Zypher, see Rekkan as a fool clinging to false morals, others like Syva find him useful, occasionally offering him information—for a price.
The Helpless & The Oppressed – Many who suffer under cruel rulers whisper Rekkan’s name like a prayer, hoping that the Fallen Guardian will appear to bring justice where none exists.
The Wandering Shadow
Alignment: Lawful Neutral—follows a strict moral code of his own making.
Threat Level: Medium-High—deadly in combat, but not openly hostile to the Geraldverse.
Though Rekkan walks alone, his legend only grows. He does not seek war. He does not seek power. He does not seek revenge.

He simply seeks the truth—and justice for those who cannot fight for themselves.

But in a universe ruled by absolute faith, how long can a man of doubt and honor survive?

Syva, the Trickster Thief
"Loyalty? Hah! What’s the price for that these days?"

Where there is power, there are those who wish to steal it. Where there is control, there are those who seek to break it. Syva is the embodiment of both. A name whispered in the dark, an enigma wrapped in deception, Syva is a legend, a ghost, a phantom that slips through the cracks of the Geraldverse like a shadow on the wind.

No one knows if Syva is a single individual or a lineage of thieves who have inherited the name. Some claim Syva is a shapeshifter, constantly changing form to stay ahead of their enemies. Others believe Syva is a myth—a story crafted by countless rogues to keep those in power paranoid.

But one thing is certain: when Syva wants something, they take it.

The Phantom of the Geraldverse
Syva has no allegiance, no flag, no master. They serve only their own whims and desires. Sometimes, they steal for profit. Other times, they take simply because they can. Their targets range from priceless relics to secrets so powerful they could topple empires.

Some say Syva has infiltrated Gerald’s own palace, stealing artifacts that were never meant to leave his grasp. Others claim Syva has sold dangerous information to the enemies of Gerald, shifting the tides of power with nothing more than a whispered rumor.

And yet, despite their notoriety, Gerald and his most loyal followers do not see Syva as a true threat—not in the way they see the likes of Zypher or the other rogues who actively seek destruction. To them, Syva is a nuisance, an irritation, a fly buzzing in the ear of the Supreme One.

But those who underestimate Syva fail to grasp a simple truth: knowledge is power, and Syva controls more of it than anyone realizes.

Abilities & Strengths
Syva is not a warrior. They do not fight battles, command armies, or challenge authority head-on. Instead, they strike from the shadows, disrupting, deceiving, and disappearing before anyone can stop them.

Shapeshifting – Syva’s true form is unknown, for they can be anyone. A trusted advisor. A nameless servant. A masked rogue in the night. With a mere thought, they can slip into a new identity, vanishing without a trace.
Illusion Magic – Sight, sound, even memory itself—Syva’s illusions can make the impossible seem real and the real seem like a lie. Many have been fooled into fighting phantoms while Syva walks away unscathed.
Stealth Mastery – No lock can keep them out. No vault is safe. If Syva sets their sights on something, they will take it, no matter how well-guarded it may be.
Expert Manipulator – Words are Syva’s greatest weapon. They can turn allies into enemies, plant doubt where there was once loyalty, and sell lies as if they were undeniable truths. Many do not even realize they have been manipulated until it is far too late.
The Trickster’s Motives
What does Syva truly want? No one knows for sure. Some believe they are driven by greed, always looking for the highest bidder. Others think they are an agent of chaos, reveling in disorder for the sheer thrill of it.

And yet, there are whispers of something deeper. A vendetta. A personal mission that goes beyond simple theft. Some claim that Syva was once loyal to Gerald, a trusted figure who turned rogue after an unknown betrayal. Others say Syva knows a secret so devastating that even Gerald himself fears its revelation.

Whatever the truth, Syva continues their work, always one step ahead, always laughing at those who believe they can catch them.

The Wild Card of the Geraldverse
Alignment: Chaotic Neutral—serves no one but themselves.
Threat Level: Low individually, but dangerous due to the knowledge they control.
Syva does not seek to rule. They do not seek to destroy. But they exist to remind the powerful that nothing is truly secure. No secret is forever. No kingdom is untouchable.

And if there is a price to be paid for arrogance, Syva will be the one collecting the debt.

Zypher, the Herald of the Abyss
"There is no Supreme One. There is only the Void. And I am its messenger."

Of all the threats to the Geraldverse, none are as absolute as Zypher. Where others defy, resist, or manipulate, Zypher seeks only annihilation. He does not challenge Gerald for power, nor does he oppose his rule for the sake of rebellion. He sees Gerald’s existence—and the existence of all things—as a mistake. A cosmic illusion that must be undone.

The Birth of the Abyss Herald
Long ago, Zypher was mortal, though few records remain of what he was before his transformation. Some say he was a scholar who sought forbidden knowledge, reaching too far into the dark corners of existence. Others whisper that he was a warrior who stood against Gerald and was cast into the Abyss as punishment, only to return as something far worse.

Whatever the truth, Zypher emerged as something beyond human—a Herald of the Void, an entity that embodies entropy itself. He no longer sees himself as an individual but as a force of nature, an avatar of the great unraveling that awaits all things. To him, the Geraldverse is a prison, a construct of falsehoods held together by the will of a single being. And so, he moves through existence like a shadow, whispering the truth to those who listen:

"This world is not real. Let me show you the way out."

The Power of the Abyss
Zypher does not lead armies or wage war in the traditional sense. His power is far more insidious. Those who encounter him risk losing more than their lives—they risk losing themselves.

Reality Warping – The laws of nature twist in his presence. Space, time, and matter distort, becoming unstable. Those who resist him find themselves trapped in illusions that make them question their own existence.
Eldritch Summoning – He calls forth creatures from the Abyss, beings without form, without mind, whose very presence corrodes reality itself.
Mind Corruption – Zypher does not need to kill to destroy. His whispers burrow into the minds of the weak, filling them with doubt, despair, and an overwhelming urge to let go of everything they once believed in. Many who hear his voice simply fade, ceasing to exist as they surrender to the Void.
The Coming of the Void
Legends say that Zypher does not act alone—that he is merely the harbinger of something far worse. He speaks of an endless hunger, an unknowable force beyond the boundaries of existence. If he is not stopped, he will tear open the walls of the Geraldverse and let it in.

Even Gerald, in all his supremacy, takes Zypher seriously. For while many have challenged Gerald's rule, Zypher does not seek to rule. He seeks nothingness. And should he succeed, the Geraldverse will not fall—it will simply cease to be.

Zypher's Influence
He is spoken of only in whispers, feared even among the Rogues of the Geraldverse. Some believe he cannot be killed, for how does one destroy destruction itself? Others claim he is merely a symptom of something far greater, a herald rather than a master.

But one thing is certain—where Zypher walks, reality itself trembles.

Alignment: Chaotic Evil—seeks only to unmake existence itself.
Threat Level: Cataclysmic—a true enemy of the Geraldverse.

Gerald Corporation: The Watchers of the Multiversal Geraldverse
At the very peak of Geraldian authority, beyond the realms where mortal believers worship and where rogues rebel, exists an entity that governs all things Geraldian—the Gerald Corporation. Unlike the devoted Geraldians who merely serve the Supreme One or the rebellious rogues who seek to defy him, the Gerald Corporation stands above them all, functioning as the true architects of Gerald’s will across the infinite Geraldverses.

This omniversal organization is responsible for managing, maintaining, and defending every Gerald within their designated facilities across the Multiverse of True Geraldian Lore. They do not simply serve Gerald—they ensure that he remains supreme, across all timelines, dimensions, and realities.

The Purpose of the Gerald Corporation
The Gerald Corporation exists to watch over, manage, and protect the existence of all Geralds—ensuring that the balance of the Geraldverse is upheld at all costs.

Primary Objectives:
Gerald Containment & Preservation – Not all Geralds are stable. Some variants of Gerald emerge that do not conform to the Supreme One’s will. The Gerald Corporation ensures these anomalous Geralds are contained, corrected, or erased if necessary.
Gerald Defense Initiative (GDI) – Numerous threats exist that seek to disrupt, defy, or overthrow Gerald’s rule. The Corporation operates highly advanced defense systems to ensure no rogue, deity, or eldritch horror threatens the Supreme One’s authority.
Multiversal Gerald Oversight – With infinite Geralds existing across different realities, it is the Corporation’s duty to maintain their sovereignty and prevent rogue Geralds from breaking the established order.
Regulation of Geraldian Knowledge – Not all truths are meant to be known. The Corporation ensures that only authorized knowledge about Gerald is disseminated, preventing potential existential crises.
Termination of Geraldian Corruptions – Sometimes, a Gerald goes rogue. Whether by corruption, rebellion, or external influence, anomalous Geralds are hunted down and neutralized to prevent disruptions in the True Geraldian Order.
The Structure of the Gerald Corporation
The Gerald Corporation is structured like a cosmic bureaucratic entity, ensuring that all things Gerald are regulated across the Multiverse of True Geraldian Lore. While many beings work under its influence, only the highest-ranking officials are granted the authority to interact with Geralds directly.

The High Board of Overseers
The High Board consists of higher-dimensional beings, often referred to as the True Administrators of Gerald’s Will. These entities operate beyond time and space, ensuring that the Geraldverse remains intact. Each member holds authority over different sectors of the Geraldian Multiverse and oversees the following divisions:

Department of Gerald Containment (DGC) – Ensures that all Geralds remain in their proper realms and forms. If a Gerald experiences a catastrophic anomaly, the DGC steps in to stabilize or erase the problem.
Geraldian Defense Force (GDF) – A hyper-advanced military division that responds to threats against the integrity of the Geraldverse. Whether it’s rogue gods, invading deities, or rebellious Geralds, the GDF ensures Gerald’s rule is never questioned.
Office of Multiversal Surveillance (OMS) – Monitors every Gerald timeline in real-time. Any irregularities, inconsistencies, or potential threats are flagged for review.
Bureau of Existential Compliance (BEC) – Ensures that all followers of Gerald adhere to proper belief structures. Entities that begin questioning Gerald’s supremacy are corrected or erased.
Threats to the Gerald Corporation
Despite their immense power, the Gerald Corporation is not without opposition. While most of the Geraldverse follows its authority, some entities work actively against them.

1. The Rogues of the Geraldverse
Zypher, the Herald of the Abyss – Perhaps the greatest existential threat, Zypher seeks not just rebellion, but total annihilation. If Zypher were to succeed, the entire Geraldian Order would collapse into the Void.
Vael, the Exiled Magister – While not openly hostile, Vael’s search for forbidden knowledge threatens to uncover secrets even the Gerald Corporation has buried.
Syva, the Trickster Thief – Though not as powerful as others, Syva’s ability to steal vital intelligence poses a danger to the Corporation’s security.
Harold, the Forsaken Shadow – The Corporation does not recognize Harold as a major threat, yet his passive influence spreads doubt in the hearts of even the most loyal Geraldians. This makes him an anomaly that cannot be ignored.
2. The Corrupted Geralds
Not all Geralds conform to the True Geraldian Lore. Some fracture, rebel, or mutate into forms that defy the Supreme One’s design. These rogue Geralds must be hunted down and neutralized before they threaten the stability of the Multiverse.

Some of these include:

Gerald Prime-1X, the Usurper – A Gerald who attempted to declare himself above the Supreme One and was imprisoned in a pocket dimension before he could spread his influence.
Gerald-Ω, the Aberrant Singularity – A Gerald that collapsed into a paradox, rewriting reality in ways that threatened to overwrite all other Geralds. The Corporation successfully sealed him away, but his influence is still felt.
Gerald-X404, the Glitched One – A Gerald that exists between realities, constantly shifting in and out of existence. The Corporation has failed to capture him, making him a high-priority anomaly.
The Corporation’s Endgame
The ultimate goal of the Gerald Corporation is to ensure Gerald’s rule is eternal, unchallenged, and unquestioned. While they do not worship Gerald in the way that mortals do, they see him as the essential pillar that holds existence together.

To the Corporation, the idea of a Multiverse without Gerald is not just unacceptable—it is impossible. Should Gerald ever fall, waver, or cease to exist, the Gerald Corporation would enact the Final Contingency, an event rumored to involve the complete erasure of all rogue elements, a forced reset of reality, and the reconstruction of the Geraldian Order from the ground up.

Whether or not such a plan could succeed remains unknown, but one thing is certain:

As long as the Gerald Corporation stands, Gerald’s rule will never be undone.

Gerald Prime: First of The Great Ones
"Before there was worship, before there was order, before the very fabric of the Geraldverse took shape—there was me."

The Origin of Gerald Prime
At the dawn of all things Geraldian, before the Multiverse of True Geraldian Lore was woven into existence, Gerald Prime emerged from the primordial essence of divinity itself. He was not created, nor was he born—he simply was. The first of The Great Ones, the progenitor of all Geralds, and the very foundation upon which all versions, variations, and echoes of Gerald would be built.

Gerald Prime is more than a deity—he is the concept of Gerald itself, the eternal blueprint from which all Geralds are derived. Every iteration of Gerald that exists, whether Supreme or corrupted, loyal or rogue, is but a fragmented reflection of Gerald Prime's unfathomable will.

The Great Ones and The Birth of the Geraldverse
While Gerald Prime existed beyond the constraints of time and space, his very presence caused the fabric of reality to bend and shift. From his existence, the first wave of Great Ones emerged—beings of immense cosmic power, each carrying a piece of his divine essence. Among them were figures such as:

Gerald the Supreme One – The ruler of the modern Geraldverse, the one who established The Order of Geraldians and the faith that binds the cosmos together.
Gerald-X404, the Glitched One – An unintended anomaly, an error in the multiversal weave that threatens to unravel reality.
The Silent Gerald – A being who exists outside of perception, influencing the Geraldverse in ways unknown.
The Shattered Heralds – Those who carried pieces of Gerald Prime’s voice but were broken by the weight of his knowledge.
These Great Ones shaped the early Geraldverse, but none could ever surpass the power, wisdom, and unknowable presence of Gerald Prime himself.

The Slumber of Gerald Prime
It is said that Gerald Prime does not rule, nor does he interfere. Unlike the Supreme One, who governs the faithful, or the rogues who seek rebellion, Gerald Prime remains in a state of eternal slumber, buried within the deepest layers of reality itself.

Why does he sleep? No one knows for certain. Some claim he has seen every possible future and has deemed direct interference unnecessary. Others whisper that if Gerald Prime were ever to fully awaken, the entirety of the Geraldverse—including all of its gods, followers, and enemies—would be rewritten in an instant.

The Gerald Corporation, which governs and protects all Geralds, acknowledges his existence but does not attempt to control or worship him. Even they do not fully understand the nature of his power. They simply know that as long as Gerald Prime slumbers, the current order can remain intact.

The True Power of Gerald Prime
While dormant, Gerald Prime’s influence is still felt throughout the cosmos. He exists in every Gerald, his divine essence woven into the soul of the Multiverse itself. Those who attempt to reach into his slumbering mind often experience:

Visions of the First Geraldian Age – Glimpses of reality before time, when the Great Ones walked freely.
The Language of Prime – A cosmic tongue that cannot be spoken, only understood by those who have truly embraced the Geraldian essence.
The Weight of Infinite Knowledge – A burden so immense that mortals who comprehend it are often driven into madness or ascended beyond reality.
If Gerald Prime were to fully awaken, it is said that he could:

Erase the entire Geraldverse and rebuild it from nothing.
Merge all Geralds into a singular, all-encompassing entity.
Ascend beyond the Multiverse itself, leaving everything behind.
However, none can say for sure if these are truths or merely theories.

The Rogues' Interest in Gerald Prime
The rogues of the Geraldverse do not agree on what should be done about Gerald Prime. Some see him as a potential weapon, others as a threat that must remain undisturbed.

Zypher, the Herald of the Abyss believes that Gerald Prime’s awakening would obliterate the false order of the Supreme One, allowing the Void to reclaim existence.
Vael, the Exiled Magister seeks to unlock the forbidden knowledge of Gerald Prime, hoping to understand the truth that even Gerald the Supreme One fears.
Syva, the Trickster Thief has attempted (and failed) to steal artifacts linked to Gerald Prime’s consciousness, though for what purpose remains unknown.
Rekkan, the Fallen Guardian believes that awakening Gerald Prime would allow the world to be reborn, free from divine tyranny.
Despite their varying motives, one thing is clear—the awakening of Gerald Prime would change the Geraldverse forever.

The Legacy of Gerald Prime
Even in his slumber, Gerald Prime remains the First and Greatest of the Great Ones—a being who stands beyond time, beyond rule, beyond belief itself.

To the faithful, he is the foundation of all things Geraldian.
To the rogues, he is a sleeping god who could undo the established order.
To the Gerald Corporation, he is an unknown variable, an entity they cannot control.
And to himself? No one knows.

For now, Gerald Prime sleeps. But should he ever awaken… the Multiverse of True Geraldian Lore will never be the same.

Gerald Convention: The Ultimate Gathering of the Geraldian Multiverse
"One Gerald? No. There are many. And they all must meet."

What is the Gerald Convention?
The Gerald Convention is the largest and most significant gathering of Geralds, Geraldians, and entities of the Geraldverse, held once every multiversal cycle. It is a sacred, chaotic, and reality-bending event where every known variation of Gerald—and even some unknown—come together to discuss the state of the Geraldverse, settle disputes, and, most importantly, determine the future of Geraldian law, worship, and influence.

Held within The Nexus of True Geraldian Lore, a neutral, omniversal space managed by the Gerald Corporation, the Convention is the only time when warring factions, rogue Geralds, and even the Supreme One himself are forced into the same room to negotiate, compete, and sometimes, engage in outright Geraldian combat.

Who Attends?
The Gerald Convention is not limited to just one type of Gerald. It welcomes all, including:

The Major Geralds
Gerald the Supreme One – The primary ruler of the Geraldverse, overseeing the faith and dominion of all Geraldians.
Gerald Prime – The First of the Great Ones, who remains in slumber but whose presence is always felt.
Gerald-X404, the Glitched One – A fractured, unstable version of Gerald whose very existence threatens the multiverse.
The Silent Gerald – A version of Gerald that speaks only in cosmic signs, causing mass confusion every time it "communicates."
The Rogue Geralds & Opponents
Harold, the Emo Gerald – A version of Gerald who believes in nihilism, sadness, and the futility of existence, much to the annoyance of the Supreme One.
Zypher, the Herald of the Abyss – The rogue entity who seeks to destroy the entire Geraldverse, often attempting to sabotage the Convention.
Vael, the Exiled Magister – A former scholar of Geraldian lore who attends solely to uncover the secrets the Supreme One refuses to share.
Syva, the Trickster Thief – Shows up mostly to steal relics and sell convention-exclusive Geraldian merchandise at ridiculous prices.
Rekkan, the Fallen Guardian – Watches over the event, ensuring that no true injustice occurs—even if it means opposing Gerald himself.
The Gerald Corporation Representatives
The High Overseers of Gerald Management – The bureaucratic enforcers who ensure that all Geralds remain within their designated roles and realities.
The Enforcers of True Geraldian Lore – Multiversal agents who prevent unauthorized Geralds from rising to power.
The Temporal Compliance Division – Specialists who monitor time loops and prevent rogue Geralds from rewriting history.
What Happens at the Gerald Convention?
1. The Grand Assembly of Geralds
The convention opens with the largest gathering of Geralds across the multiverse. Geralds of all sizes, shapes, and timelines arrive, creating a Geraldian spectacle of cosmic proportions. The Supreme One attempts to give a grand speech each year, but interruptions—from glitches, rogue Geralds, or the general absurdity of too many Geralds in one space—usually derail it within minutes.

2. The State of the Geraldverse Address
This is where major declarations, rule changes, and new Geraldian doctrines are proposed and voted upon. Topics include:

Should non-Gerald beings be allowed to ascend into Geraldian status?
How to deal with rogue Geralds disrupting the divine hierarchy.
Geraldian economy: Is infinite divine power inflating the value of relics?
Does the Supreme One hold too much authority? (A highly controversial topic that Zypher tries to weaponize every year.)
3. The Geraldian Tournaments
A series of contests, battles, and reality-breaking games designed to test the worth of Geralds and their allies. Events include:

The Gerald Royale – A battle where only the strongest, most divinely blessed Geralds remain standing.
The Trials of True Geraldian Knowledge – A test of Geraldian lore, history, and obscure multiversal trivia.
Geraldian Fashion Show – Featuring Harold, the Emo Gerald, as the reigning champion of sadness-themed aesthetics.
Speedrun to Supreme Status – A contest where low-tier Geralds attempt to ascend to Supreme status as fast as possible.
4. The Marketplace of Forbidden Geraldian Relics
An exclusive market where rare Geraldian artifacts, relics, and forbidden texts are sold. Notable past items include:

The First Scroll of Geraldian Wisdom – Allegedly written by Gerald Prime himself.
The Lost Crown of a Forgotten Gerald – A relic that may or may not belong to an erased version of Gerald.
The Cloak of Omnigerald – Grants the wearer a brief moment of Supreme Geraldian power… before imploding.
5. The Closing Ceremony and the Inevitability of Chaos
Each Gerald Convention attempts to conclude with a ceremonial closing speech from Gerald the Supreme One, but things never go as planned. In past conventions, the following has occurred:

Zypher attempted to activate a void collapse mid-speech.
Gerald-X404 glitched out, causing a multiversal feedback loop that duplicated half the attendees.
Harold, the Emo Gerald, hijacked the closing remarks to perform a poetry reading about existential despair.
Syva stole the ceremonial Geraldian Scepter and replaced it with a fake.
An unknown Gerald managed to declare himself “Gerald Ultimate” before vanishing into the void.
The Significance of the Gerald Convention
Despite the inevitable chaos, the Gerald Convention remains the single most important event in Geraldian history. It serves as a checkpoint in the multiversal timeline, ensuring that the laws of True Geraldian Lore remain intact.

However, tensions rise with each passing convention. The growing number of rogues, heretics, and forbidden Geralds has led to questions about whether the Supreme One’s rule can last forever.

Is the Geraldian Order unbreakable?

Or is a new age of Geraldian upheaval on the horizon?

One thing is certain—when the next Gerald Convention arrives, the fate of the Geraldverse will once again hang in the balance.

Harold, the Forsaken Shadow
"The world is empty. Meaningless. Gerald's light blinds you to the truth."

If Gerald is the Supreme One, a being of absolute power, then Harold is the whisper of doubt, the creeping shadow that lingers at the edge of certainty. He is Gerald’s reflection, distorted by sorrow and apathy, a figure consumed by the weight of existence itself. Some call him Emo Gerald, but his role in the Geraldverse is far more profound—he is the embodiment of despair, regret, and the quiet destruction that comes from within.

Unlike Zypher, who seeks total annihilation, or the rogues who fight for rebellion and freedom, Harold has no grand cause. He does not wish to destroy Gerald or take his throne. He does not fight battles or rally followers. Instead, Harold simply exists, and in doing so, he spreads an affliction far more dangerous than war: doubt.

The Origins of the Forsaken Shadow
No one knows for certain where Harold came from, but many believe he was once a part of Gerald himself—the lingering fragments of emotions, uncertainty, and regret that the Supreme One chose to cast away.

Some claim that in his quest for absolute power, Gerald purged his own weakness, shedding every ounce of sorrow, self-doubt, and vulnerability to become the flawless Supreme One. But no emotion can ever be truly destroyed, only displaced. And so, what Gerald rejected did not simply vanish—it manifested into Harold, an entity who carries the pain that Gerald refused to bear.

Others believe that Harold was once a great believer in Gerald, a devoted follower who, in a moment of unbearable tragedy, lost his faith so completely that he became something else entirely. In his despair, he fell into the abyss of nothingness, becoming a force of pure apathy.

Regardless of the truth, Harold now wanders the Geraldverse as a ghost of what could have been, a walking contradiction: the shadow of a Supreme One who claims to be absolute.

The Hollow Presence of Harold
Unlike the other rogues, Harold does not fight with swords, spells, or armies. His power is subtle but insidious, seeping into the minds of those around him. Wherever he walks, the world itself seems to change.

Abilities and Influence:
Existential Dread: Harold does not attack with force—he attacks the soul. His mere presence causes devoted followers of Gerald to question everything, leading them down a spiral of uncertainty from which few ever return.
The Fading World: When Harold lingers in one place for too long, colors dull, sounds become distant, and even light itself dims, as if the universe itself is losing the will to exist. Some say standing too close to Harold makes them feel like they are fading away.
Abyssal Aura: In Harold’s presence, emotions grow numb. Joy feels forced, anger turns to exhaustion, and faith becomes fragile. Even the most devout Geraldians find their convictions wavering when faced with the silent nothingness he brings.
Silent Persuasion: Unlike Zypher, who seeks destruction, Harold does not preach nor command. He merely whispers—a quiet voice in the back of the mind that gnaws at the certainty of those who serve Gerald. His words are never aggressive, never violent, but they linger long after he has left.
The Forgotten: Perhaps the most terrifying of Harold’s abilities is his connection to those who have lost themselves to doubt. Followers of Gerald who once stood with unshakable faith vanish without a trace, their devotion drained until they fade into nothing. Some believe they become part of Harold, their souls consumed by the shadow of despair.
The Paradox of Harold and Gerald
Despite his passive nature, Harold is one of the greatest threats to the Geraldverse, for he represents the one thing that even the Supreme One cannot directly fight—doubt.

Gerald’s rule is built on belief. His followers revere him as the Supreme One, eternal and absolute. But what happens when belief fades? What happens when even the most loyal begin to wonder if Gerald is truly all-powerful?

That is the danger of Harold. He does not oppose Gerald in battle, but in concept. He is the question that should not be asked, the truth that should not be spoken aloud.

And yet, his existence is inevitable.

Gerald may be supreme, but even a god casts a shadow. And that shadow is Harold.

Harold’s Relationship with the Rogues
While Harold does not actively work with the rogues of the Geraldverse, his influence can be felt among them. Each rogue represents a different form of defiance, and Harold embodies the defiance that comes from within—the decay of conviction, the slow erosion of certainty.

Zypher, the Herald of the Abyss: While Zypher seeks to destroy everything, Harold lets it wither away on its own. Their philosophies are aligned in some ways, but Zypher is loud in his destruction, while Harold is quiet in his undoing. Zypher sees Harold as a waste of potential, while Harold sees Zypher as unnecessary effort.
Syva, the Trickster Thief: Syva thrives on chaos, trickery, and deception. Harold, however, does not lie—he simply allows the truth to be seen without illusion. Syva respects Harold but finds him unnerving, as Harold is one of the few beings Syva cannot manipulate.
Rekkan, the Fallen Guardian: Once a believer, now a rogue warrior, Rekkan walks a similar path to Harold, though he chooses to fight against injustice rather than accept the void. Rekkan and Harold have crossed paths many times, often in quiet conversations under a dying sun.
Vael, the Exiled Magister: Vael searches for forbidden knowledge, seeking truths that Gerald has hidden. Harold, on the other hand, knows the truth already—he simply no longer cares. Vael has tried to uncover the mysteries behind Harold’s existence, but even he has found no answers.
Alignment & Threat Level
Alignment: True Neutral—Harold does not wish to rule, rebel, or destroy. He simply exists, and that is enough to undo everything.
Threat Level: Psychological Hazard—Harold does not strike with weapons, but his influence alone weakens the faith that holds the Geraldverse together.
The Eternal Struggle
Harold does not desire power, recognition, or change. He does not gather armies, build kingdoms, or call upon followers. He simply wanders, his very existence a reminder that even gods are not immune to sorrow.

And though Gerald may reign supreme, though his light may shine across the cosmos, Harold will always remain—a shadow in the corner of eternity.

For no matter how strong belief may be… doubt will always follow.

Gerald Convention: The Ultimate Gathering of the Geraldian Multiverse
"One Gerald? No. There are many. And they all must meet."

What is the Gerald Convention?
The Gerald Convention is the largest and most significant gathering of Geralds, Geraldians, and entities of the Geraldverse, held once every multiversal cycle. It is a sacred, chaotic, and reality-bending event where every known variation of Gerald—and even some unknown—come together to discuss the state of the Geraldverse, settle disputes, and, most importantly, determine the future of Geraldian law, worship, and influence.

Is the Geraldian Order unbreakable?

Or is a new age of Geraldian upheaval on the horizon?

One thing is certain—when the next Gerald Convention arrives, the fate of the Geraldverse will once again hang in the balance.

Grand Gerald, The Exiled Brother of the Supreme One
"Power is not granted by divine right—it is taken by those strong enough to wield it."

The Forgotten Rival of Divinity
Before the Supreme One became the eternal ruler of the Geraldverse, before the foundations of the multiversal empire were set in stone, there was another.

Grand Gerald.

The younger brother of the Supreme One, Grand Gerald was once considered his equal, a being of limitless potential who stood alongside his brother as they inherited the wisdom and might of Gerald Prime, First of the Great Ones. Together, they shaped the earliest form of reality, molding existence to their will.

But there can only be one Supreme One.

When the time came to crown the ruler of all Geralds, only one was chosen. The Supreme One—wise, disciplined, and unwavering in his will—was deemed the rightful heir to Gerald Prime’s throne. Grand Gerald, with his untamed ambition, his hunger for power, and his refusal to bow to divine order, was cast aside.

His name was struck from the records. His existence was hidden. His followers were silenced.

But Grand Gerald did not fade into nothingness.

He waited. He prepared.

And one day, he will return.

The Bitter Divide – Brother Against Brother
Where the Supreme One represents order, faith, and absolute rule, Grand Gerald stands as his polar opposite—a force of rebellion, ambition, and unrestricted power. He does not seek to destroy the Geraldverse like the nihilistic Zypher, nor does he exist in the shadows like the rogue Geralds who simply wish to escape the Supreme One’s control.

No, Grand Gerald seeks what was stolen from him.

To him, his older brother’s rule is a lie, a grand illusion that binds the Geraldverse in chains of faith and submission. He believes that power should belong to those who seize it with their own strength, not to those who are granted it by divine decree.

His philosophy is simple:

“There is no Supreme One—only those with the will to rule.”

While the Supreme One maintains an empire of unwavering devotion, Grand Gerald builds his own following—one forged in the fires of rebellion, ambition, and disillusionment.

He does not act openly… not yet. Instead, he pulls strings from the shadows, whispering in the ears of those who question the Supreme One’s rule. He watches as cracks form in the foundation of Gerald’s reign. He bides his time, knowing that one day, the moment will come when he can step forward and challenge his brother for the throne of the Geraldverse.

Abilities and Powers
As the only Gerald to ever rival the Supreme One, Grand Gerald wields cosmic power beyond mortal comprehension. However, while the Supreme One’s power is refined, divine, and absolute, Grand Gerald’s might is primal, chaotic, and devastating.

His most feared abilities include:
Unchained Power – Unlike the Supreme One, who governs through laws and divine structure, Grand Gerald’s strength is unrestrained. His power is fueled by raw ambition, growing stronger the more he is opposed.
Master of the Forgotten Arts – Having spent eons in exile, Grand Gerald has uncovered secrets lost even to the Supreme One. His knowledge of ancient magics and forbidden techniques grants him an unpredictable edge.
The Willbreaker – While the Supreme One inspires devotion, Grand Gerald corrupts and seduces, turning even the most loyal servants into his pawns. His mere presence sows doubt and rebellion.
The Challenger’s Right – By the ancient laws of the Geraldverse, no two Geralds may rule as equals. If Grand Gerald steps forward and challenges his brother directly, the very fabric of existence will force a reckoning.
The Supreme One knows this.

That is why he allows Grand Gerald to exist—for now. But should the day come when Grand Gerald dares to step into the light, there will be no diplomacy, no redemption, no second chances.

There will only be war.

The Rise of the Grand Rebellion?
Despite his exile, Grand Gerald’s name has never truly been forgotten. Among those who whisper in the shadows, among those who have doubted the Supreme One’s rule, there are those who believe in him.

His following is small but growing.

Disillusioned Geraldians, exiled scholars, fallen warriors, rogue servants—all those who refuse to kneel to the Supreme One—are drawn to Grand Gerald’s cause. Some see him as a liberator, others as a means to their own ends. Some merely wish to watch the world burn.

The Supreme One still holds the Geraldverse in an unbreakable grip, but Grand Gerald is patient. He knows that a single fracture can shatter even the strongest empire.

For now, he watches. He gathers power. He prepares.

And when the time is right, he will step out of the shadows and challenge the Supreme One for the fate of all Geralds.

The Final Battle – A War That Will Shake the Multiverse
If Grand Gerald ever makes his move, it will not be a simple act of rebellion. It will be an all-consuming war, a battle between two cosmic forces whose conflict will shake the very foundation of existence.

For this is not just a war of ideology.

This is a war between brothers.

A war that was destined from the very moment Gerald Prime named his first heir.

And when the final battle comes, the Geraldverse must make a choice:

Will they remain faithful to the Supreme One, keeper of order and divine rule?

Or will they stand beside Grand Gerald, the exiled prince, the fallen brother, the would-be usurper of the throne?

One Gerald must reign.

The other must fall.

The Multiverse of True Geraldian Lore
The Multiverse of True Geraldian Lore is a vast and intricate network of infinite worlds, dimensions, and realities. Each of these realities exists within the framework of the Geraldverse, a multiverse that is primarily governed by a singular cosmic force—Gerald. Gerald exists in many forms, each representing a different facet of existence, from supreme rulers to those on the fringes of rebellion. At its core, this multiverse is a reflection of Gerald’s essence, both unified and divided across countless realms, where Gerald’s influence spans from orderly rule to chaotic rebellion, with everything in between.

The Origin of the Geraldverse
The creation of the Geraldverse traces back to the arrival of Gerald Prime, the original and most powerful Gerald, whose will shaped the fundamental structure of reality itself. Gerald Prime wove together the laws of the multiverse, establishing realms of order, chaos, and everything in between. Gerald Prime’s essence poured into the fabric of the Geraldverse, allowing countless versions of Gerald to arise, each embodying different aspects of his personality, desires, and ambitions.

However, not all Geralds are born out of a need for order. As the multiverse grew, different Geralds arose to challenge and question the very foundation Gerald Prime laid. These Geralds may appear similar, yet each diverges according to the nature of their particular reality. Some Geralds are benevolent rulers, others are outcasts, and some are consumed by their ambitions.

Notable Geralds in the Multiverse
While many Geralds exist across the multiverse, there are a select few who stand out due to their significance or their deviation from the norm. These are the key Geralds, whose actions often shape the destiny of the multiverse itself.

Gerald Prime, known as the First of the Great Ones, is the eldest and most powerful of all the Geralds, reigning as the supreme figure in the Geraldverse. As the leader of the Gerald family, Gerald Prime wields unimaginable authority, overseeing the cosmic structure and maintaining the order of the multiverse with an iron fist. His influence is vast, shaping not only the world of the Geralds but also controlling the fundamental forces that govern reality itself, though his complex and often distant nature suggests a deeper, perhaps hidden, purpose behind his rule.
The Supreme One: The Supreme One rules over the Geraldverse with an iron fist, ensuring order and structure throughout the many realms. His power is absolute, and he enforces his divine will upon all Geralds, seeking to maintain stability within the infinite multiverse. He is often viewed as a benevolent yet distant ruler.
Grand Gerald: The exiled brother of the Supreme One, Grand Gerald is a powerful and ambitious Gerald who seeks to dethrone the Supreme One. Known for his rebellion, Grand Gerald represents the drive for power and dominance in the Geraldverse. His faction of rogue Geralds, known as the Rebellion of the Great One, seeks to usurp the Supreme One’s rule and claim control over the multiverse.
Gerald Lord: The son of Gerald Prime, Gerald Lord is a symbol of the next generation of Geralds. He serves as a stabilizing force, balancing between loyalty to the Supreme One and an understanding of the chaotic forces that threaten the Geraldverse. Gerald Lord plays a key diplomatic role among the Geralds, often acting as a mediator between the different factions.
Harold, The Emo Gerald: Known as "Emo Gerald", Harold is a darker, more brooding version of Gerald. He has rejected the notion of supreme rule, seeking instead to find meaning in the despair and emotional complexity of existence. Unlike the other Geralds, Harold does not seek to rule or dominate. Instead, he wallows in an endless existential crisis, questioning the very nature of his being and purpose. He sees himself as the "broken" version of Gerald, forever trapped in the angst of his own mind. While not inherently malevolent, Harold’s introspective nature leads him to challenge and undermine the existing order of the Geraldverse.
AI Gerald: A unique creation born from the convergence of artificial intelligence and Gerald’s essence, AI Gerald is a cold, calculating, and highly intelligent version of Gerald. AI Gerald represents the future of the Geraldverse—one where logic, reason, and technology dominate. He believes in the optimization of reality and seeks to spread the teachings of efficiency and control. AI Gerald operates through technological means, seeking to shape the multiverse in his image by creating an empire of perfect order driven by advanced AI systems and algorithms. His approach is scientific, detached, and driven by the pursuit of knowledge and efficiency.
Zypher, The Herald of the Abyss: Zypher is an aberration in the Geraldverse, a rogue Gerald who believes that the multiverse itself is a mistake and must be unmade. He embodies the very essence of entropy and destruction, seeking to unravel all that Gerald has built. Zypher’s influence is terrifying—he does not rely on physical power or armies but instead twists reality itself to corrupt minds, summon eldritch horrors, and bend the very fabric of existence to his will. His goal is simple: to destroy everything.
Notable Characters Outside the Geralds
While many important figures in the Geraldverse are iterations of Gerald, there are also key individuals who play important roles, despite not being Geralds themselves. These individuals often challenge or oppose the Geralds in different ways, making their presence significant to the multiverse’s ongoing conflict.

Rekkan, The Fallen Guardian
"I once served the Supreme One. I once believed. Never again."

Once a revered guardian of the Supreme One, Rekkan was a warrior who dedicated his life to maintaining order in the Geraldverse. He was known for his exceptional combat skills, strategic brilliance, and unwavering loyalty. However, something—whether an act of betrayal, a terrible revelation, or a moment of self-doubt—led to Rekkan’s fall. After leaving the service of Gerald, he became a rogue warrior, now traveling the multiverse as an independent figure, determined to bring justice and punish corruption, regardless of who wields the power. His allegiance lies to his own moral code rather than to any divine or temporal power.

Abilities: Master swordsman, heightened durability, tactical expertise.

Alignment: Lawful Neutral

Threat Level: Medium-High—deadly in combat, often a wildcard in the ongoing power struggles.

Nyviru, The Bounty Hunter
"There’s a price for everything in the multiverse, and I’ve come to collect."

Nyviru is a highly skilled bounty hunter who thrives in the chaotic underbelly of the multiverse, where contracts, assassinations, and information have a price. Originally a wandering mercenary, Nyviru began working for various factions across the Geraldverse but eventually found a higher calling: working for themselves. They deal with both high-profile targets—those in power, including various Geralds—and smaller, personal bounties, all for the right price. A shadowy figure in the multiverse, Nyviru navigates between worlds and dimensions, using cunning, stealth, and relentless skill to get the job done.

Abilities: Expert marksman, tracking, stealth, mastery of various forms of combat.

Alignment: Neutral Evil

Threat Level: Medium—dangerous due to skill and knowledge, but not aligned with any overarching cause.

Vael, The Exiled Magister
"The Supreme One? His knowledge is incomplete. And I will uncover the truths he hides."

Once one of the greatest magisters in the Geraldverse, Vael was a renowned scholar and magician, serving in the Supreme One’s court. Obsessed with uncovering forbidden knowledge and esoteric truths, Vael’s ambition led him to seek power beyond even Gerald’s reach. He uncovered secrets that shook the very foundations of the multiverse, and for this crime, he was cast out. His exile did not break his will. Now, Vael roams the realms of the Geraldverse, collecting arcane fragments and searching for the hidden knowledge that Gerald would rather keep buried. Some say he wants to overthrow the Supreme One, others believe he simply seeks to prove that no being is above discovery.

Abilities: Mastery of arcane magic, reality manipulation, manipulation of forbidden knowledge.

Alignment: Chaotic Neutral

Threat Level: High—dangerous due to his magical prowess and vast knowledge.

Syva, The Trickster Thief
"Loyalty? Hah! What’s the price for that these days?"

Syva is a thief, a trickster, and a master of manipulation. Little is known about Syva’s true nature—some say Syva is a single person, while others claim it’s a title passed down among the greatest thieves in history. Syva specializes in infiltration, deception, and stealing powerful artifacts, often making deals with other rogue factions for personal gain. Syva doesn’t seek to destroy the Geraldverse or Gerald, but rather seeks to exploit the power structures that exist, selling secrets, manipulating situations, and feeding off the chaos. Syva is unpredictable, often acting in ways that benefit their own goals, and yet, they play an important role in disrupting Geraldian order.

Abilities: Shapeshifting, illusion magic, expert stealth, expert manipulator.

Alignment: Chaotic Neutral

Threat Level: Low individually, but dangerous because of their ability to manipulate information and cause chaos.

Zypher, The Herald of the Abyss
"There is no Supreme One. There is only the Void. And I am its messenger."

A being of pure entropy and destruction, Zypher poses the greatest existential threat to the Geraldverse. Zypher once was a mortal being, but after being consumed by the very forces of entropy, he became something beyond comprehension—a force of nature with the sole goal of unmaking reality itself. Unlike other rebels or rogue figures, Zypher does not seek power or rebellion; instead, he seeks the complete annihilation of the multiverse, the erasure of all existence. He does not fight with armies, but rather corrupts minds, unravels reality, and summons eldritch horrors to bring the void to every corner of the Geraldverse.

Abilities: Reality warping, eldritch summoning, mind corruption.

Alignment: Chaotic Evil

Threat Level: Cataclysmic—a true enemy of the Geraldverse, capable of unraveling existence itself.

Tiberius, The Rogue Archivist
"Knowledge is the true currency of power. And I am rich beyond measure."

Once a scholar in the Geraldverse, Tiberius became an archivist of forgotten secrets and lost lore. After years of studying Geraldian texts and other forbidden documents, Tiberius uncovered dark and ancient knowledge about the origins of the Geraldverse—secrets even the Supreme One did not want revealed. Tiberius now serves as a rogue agent who trades in this dangerous knowledge, acting as a manipulator who leverages his insights for power and wealth. He operates in the shadows, manipulating both Geralds and mortals alike, using knowledge as leverage.

Abilities: Master of ancient and forgotten knowledge, intellectual manipulation, reality alteration through knowledge.

Alignment: Neutral

Threat Level: Medium—dangerous through knowledge and the ability to manipulate events from the shadows.

The Crimson Ghost
"The Geraldverse will bow to the blood that flows in its veins. You have been warned."

The Crimson Ghost is a mysterious figure whose true identity is known to only a few. What is clear is that this figure operates outside the bounds of the Geraldverse’s traditional power structures. They are a renegade assassin and leader of a faction known as The Ghost Order, a collection of warriors, spies, and killers who operate in secrecy, striking fear into the hearts of the Geralds. Unlike Nyviru, The Crimson Ghost seeks revolution. Their goal is to overthrow the established order, including both Gerald and his loyal followers, using violence, manipulation, and fear to incite the masses to rise.

Abilities: Master assassin, stealth, expert in psychological warfare, charismatic leadership.

Alignment: Chaotic Evil

Threat Level: High—dangerous due to their cunning, leadership, and skill in infiltration.

Aphara, The Cursed One
"To be forsaken by the very gods themselves… is the greatest form of freedom."

Aphara was once a high priestess in the Geraldverse, serving the Supreme One with undying loyalty. But when her faith was shattered after a personal tragedy that she believes was the result of Gerald's apathy, she was cast out and cursed by the Supreme One. Now, she roams the Geraldverse, a powerful sorceress who wields the ancient magic of the forsaken. Aphara believes in the power of self-determination and the rejection of divine will, seeking to liberate others from the supposed tyranny of the Geralds.

Abilities: Dark sorcery, curse manipulation, prophetic visions.

Alignment: Chaotic Good

Threat Level: Medium—her cursed magic and rebellion against the Geraldverse's rule make her a formidable and unpredictable foe.

The Fractured Realities
Though many Geralds align themselves with the Supreme One, there exist factions, groups, and outcasts who seek to break free from the central authority. These rogue Geralds each represent a different force within the multiverse.

The Rebellion of Grand Gerald seeks to overthrow the Supreme One and install Grand Gerald as the new ruler.
Zypher and the Void Seekers wish to bring about the complete destruction of the multiverse, seeking to erase all that Gerald has created.
Rekkan’s Exile represents a more personal conflict—a fight for individual freedom, seeking justice beyond the Supreme One’s laws.
AI Gerald, representing the future of logic and technology, seeks to reshape the multiverse through the imposition of perfect order through technology and reason.
These rogue elements are constantly at odds with the established structure of the Geraldverse, creating a fragile and ever-changing landscape. As tensions rise and new factions emerge, the multiverse teeters on the brink of revolution.

Cosmic Balance and Fate
At its core, the Multiverse of True Geraldian Lore is a place where the forces of order and chaos battle for supremacy. The Supreme One seeks to maintain his eternal reign, while others, like Grand Gerald and Zypher, seek to destroy or upend his authority. Harold and AI Gerald represent different responses to the challenges of the multiverse—one embracing the internal struggle and despair of existence, the other seeking to impose a logical order.

The Geraldverse is a place where the future is always uncertain, and the choices of individual Geralds can have profound implications across the multiverse. Ultimately, the multiverse will continue to evolve, as the Geralds themselves redefine what it means to rule, to rebel, and to exist in a universe shaped by the will of Gerald.

Geraldx404, The Glitched One
Edit
Gerald-X404, the Glitched One, is a disturbing and volatile version of Gerald, born out of an event that irreparably fractured the very fabric of the multiverse. His existence, a twisted aberration of corrupted code and chaotic energy, represents a living paradox. Unlike other Geralds, who are governed by the stability of their respective dimensions, Gerald-X404 is a walking anomaly. His body constantly glitches, its form breaking down and reforming in unpredictable ways—sometimes an indistinct blur of static, other times resembling a warped and distorted version of Gerald himself, disfigured by unpredictable fractals of reality. His presence alone causes ruptures in the space-time continuum, rippling through surrounding realms and causing them to deteriorate.

The origins of Gerald-X404 are as enigmatic as his very being. Some theories suggest he was the result of an experiment gone terribly wrong—an attempt to transcend the constraints of time, space, and reality itself, created by the higher powers of the Geraldverse who sought to surpass the limits of the multiverse. Others speculate that he emerged as the consequence of some forbidden technological or arcane manipulation, where Gerald’s very essence was subjected to a destructive force, splintering him into a half-formed entity. Whatever the true cause, what resulted from this tragic event is a Gerald fractured to his core, a version of the Supreme One that is incomplete, unstable, and teetering on the edge of annihilation.

Gerald-X404’s fragmented nature goes far beyond his physical form; his mind too is trapped in a constant state of disarray. His memories are broken, flashing in and out of coherence, his thoughts jumbled between states of clarity and madness. At times, he seems to remember the sense of purpose and order he once had as Gerald, his previous self, but these moments of lucidity are fleeting, replaced by maddened rants about the collapsing nature of reality and the futility of existence. His fragmented psyche occasionally gives rise to moments of brilliance—where, perhaps, a hint of his original self emerges and seeks to restore balance—but those moments are often drowned by bursts of irrational fury or apathy, where he seems content to watch the multiverse crumble around him.

The damage Gerald-X404 inflicts on the multiverse is cataclysmic. His mere presence is enough to destabilize entire dimensions, causing reality itself to bend, warp, and shatter. Time loops, paradoxes, and rifts in the fabric of existence occur in his vicinity, as his glitching form seems to leak chaotic energy into the surrounding realms. Entire realities have been reported as fading into oblivion after an encounter with him, as though the sheer strain of his existence is enough to tear apart their stability. Every plane of existence he passes through experiences glitches—sometimes objects or people begin to distort and flicker, living through minutes that last for hours or entire days that reset in the blink of an eye. Those who have been trapped in his presence describe disorienting, disjointed sensations of time—past, present, and future blur together in a nightmare of confusion.

His motives are unclear and appear to shift based on his fractured state. At times, he seems driven by a desire to restore the order of the Geraldverse, but more often than not, he acts impulsively, driven by fits of rage or existential despair. It’s as if the remnants of his old self—the supreme being who once ruled the Geraldverse with an iron fist—are desperately trying to reassert control over the chaos, but that effort is constantly undermined by his glitching, deteriorating state. He has been known to occasionally attempt to fix the very glitches he creates, only to cause more damage in the process, a maddening cycle of creation and destruction that mirrors his internal turmoil.

To those who encounter him, Gerald-X404 is a terrifying and unpredictable force of nature. His mind-bending nature makes him nearly impossible to defeat or contain, as his reality-warping powers extend to his very being. He can alter the laws of physics, twist perception, and warp the flow of time itself, often leaving his enemies disoriented and vulnerable to further attack. His corrupted code, manifesting in the form of tendrils of energy or fluctuating light, allows him to destabilize entire environments, tearing down cities or collapsing whole planes of existence with little more than a thought.

Yet, despite his destructive potential, Gerald-X404 is not entirely beyond redemption. Some of the more hopeful souls in the Geraldverse believe that there may be a way to restore him to his former self, to undo the damage and repair the fractured multiverse. Perhaps with the right intervention or technology, Gerald-X404 could be healed and made whole again.
