Origins of the Meme: The Tale of Gerald-Polar
The origins of the Polar Bear Walking Meme trace back to a long-forgotten experiment conducted by an enigmatic Gerald known as Gerald-Polar. Gerald-Polar, unlike other Geralds who were typically formed through processes of metaphysical manipulation or cosmic experimentation, was a fusion of the primordial and the paradoxical. Created through an obscure experiment blending animalistic instincts with the transcendent powers of a Geraldian being, Gerald-Polar became something wholly unique: a creature of both animal and cosmic consciousness, embodying an essence of pure instinct and divine absurdity.

Gerald-Polar's strange form was an unholy amalgamation of bear-like bulk and human intellect, granting him both remarkable power and an awkward, lumbering grace. However, despite his immense abilities and the profound energy coursing through him, he carried an aura of indifference, strolling through the cosmic chaos as though he was completely oblivious to the destruction and turmoil unfolding around him.

At one particular moment, as Gerald-Polar wandered along the shores of a desolate, forgotten world—its sky swirling with rifts, stars collapsing, and realities fracturing—an eternal gif was born. The image captured Gerald-Polar walking steadily along a beach, his polar bear body moving with an almost hypnotic, languid gait, unfazed by the collapsing universe surrounding him. This serene walk, unmarred by the cosmic catastrophe enveloping him, became an iconic visual expression of one essential truth: sometimes, nothing really matters.

The image soon found its way into the hearts of those within the Geraldian underworld—who were quick to recognize in it a strangely powerful symbol. It came to represent a nonchalant acceptance of the absurdity that is the core of Geraldian existence, where even the most tumultuous of events can seem to fade into irrelevance with the right attitude. The meme became an artifact of existential humor, a reminder that chaos and order are fleeting concepts, and in the end, nothing truly matters except one's ability to simply walk forward.

The Role of the Meme in the Geraldverse
Within the complex systems of the Geraldian Management, corporate bureaucracy, and the multiversal rifts, the Polar Bear Walking Meme holds an odd, yet important role in the collective psyche of Geralds and their higher-ups. It is frequently invoked in moments of existential crisis or cosmic imbalance, where Geralds face the inevitability of their chaotic universe. As a meme, it acts as both a coping mechanism and a reminder of what truly matters.

In the High Overlookers’ Halls:
It is said that high-ranking officials within the Gerald Corporation—beings responsible for the delicate balance of the Geraldverse—often turn to the gif as a form of mediation before making weighty decisions. The image of Gerald-Polar’s relaxed stride serves as a calming influence, helping them regain focus and perspective, especially during moments when the responsibilities of maintaining order seem overwhelming.

The meme has even been said to inspire the most successful decision-making within the Gerald Management Division, offering a reminder that chaos is inevitable, but one must embrace the chaos, walking through it without concern for its infinite dimensions. The gif’s serene loop encourages them to let go of unnecessary worry and approach their monumental tasks with the same detached grace as Gerald-Polar.

During Moments of Cosmic Crisis:
The meme frequently resurfaces during the most calamitous crises in the Geraldverse. Whether it is the arrival of Gerald-X404, a fractured Gerald threatening to erase all existence, or the appearance of an eldritch cosmic horror that defies comprehension, the Polar Bear Walking Gif serves as a paradoxical form of comfort. In the face of the impossible, the absurdity of the universe, and the chaos of existence, it reminds those who view it that, while the universe may seem like a place of endless catastrophe and confusion, there is a choice—to walk through it unfazed.

Geralds, upon encountering moments of galactic annihilation or dimensional collapse, have been known to pull up the gif on their cosmic monitors to calm their minds, take a deep breath, and allow themselves to be reminded of their smallness in the face of the unfathomable vastness of the Geraldverse.

Cultural Impact and Legacy:
The meme’s influence goes far beyond mere humor. It has become a cultural touchstone among those who reject rigid notions of order and chaos alike. In factions that seek to break free from the constraints of traditional power structures, the gif is a symbol of rebellion—a reminder that even in defiance, there is grace in the way one moves through the turbulence of existence.

The meme’s spiritual resonance is felt particularly among those who question the meaning of the Geraldverse and their place within it. Spiritual seekers, philosophers, and chaos theorists within the Geraldian cultures look to the polar bear’s stride as a metaphor for divine indifference. This meme challenges their beliefs about fate, free will, and cosmic order, as it presents a worldview where all things are both infinitely significant and entirely meaningless.

The Enduring Legacy of Gerald-Polar:
While the original Gerald-Polar—the being responsible for this gif—disappeared from the known Geraldverse some time ago, his influence lives on. Some say that he ascended to a higher plane of existence, becoming a being of pure cosmic consciousness, forever walking the multiverses in timeless reflection. Others believe that Gerald-Polar simply wanders between realities, still carrying with him the air of unfazed serenity that gave birth to the meme.

Regardless of the truth, it is said that whenever a Gerald faces insurmountable odds, they may find themselves visited by the ghostly image of Gerald-Polar, walking through a cosmic void, his calm gaze locked onto them as a reminder: Walk forward, unperturbed, and let the chaos flow around you.

This perpetual legacy of Gerald-Polar ensures that the Polar Bear Walking Gif remains a timeless symbol of apathy, transcendence, and the ability to walk through the madness of existence—undisturbed, undaunted, and eternally nonchalant.

Thus, the **gif lives on as a sacred icon, forever immortalized as a lighthearted reminder to those navigating the chaos of the Geraldverse that sometimes, the best response to the crushing weight of reality is simply to keep walking forward.

Isekai Protagonist Gerald – The Chosen One of Infinite Realities
"I didn't choose this fate… but I sure as hell won't waste it."

The Accidental Hero of the Geraldverse
In a multiverse dominated by powerful Geralds, bureaucratic deities, and cosmic-scale institutions, one entity stands out—not because of his experience, divine lineage, or established power, but because he was never supposed to be here in the first place.

Isekai Protagonist Gerald is a living anomaly, a being who was not born within the Geraldverse, nor created by any of its many cosmic systems. Unlike the Supreme One, the High Overseers, or the Gerald Corporation, he was never intended to have a role in the grand structure of existence. Instead, he was violently and inexplicably summoned from another world—a mundane, powerless existence—into the chaotic reality of True Geraldian Lore.

Most Geralds are either engineered through divine experimentation, ascended through cosmic inheritance, or spawned from fundamental aspects of reality itself. But Isekai Protagonist Gerald? He was just an ordinary human in an ordinary world. A nobody.

Then, in an instant, he became everything.

Summoning & The "Fate-Breaking Incident"
The event that brought Isekai Protagonist Gerald into the Geraldverse is a cosmic mystery. Unlike other "transported souls" who are usually guided by divine will or summoned by powerful beings, his arrival was completely unplanned. No records exist within the Gerald Corporation's interdimensional archives detailing his emergence, and no faction or deity has stepped forward to claim responsibility.

Some believe he was the result of a reality malfunction, an accident caused by an error in the Temporal Compliance Division's monitoring systems. Others claim a dying god from outside the Geraldverse summoned him, channeling all of its remaining power to bring forth a hero from beyond existence.

A more radical theory suggests that Isekai Protagonist Gerald summoned himself—that something deep within his soul resonated with the infinite chaos of the multiverse, pulling him across dimensions through sheer force of will.

Regardless of the cause, his sudden arrival sent ripples through reality itself. His very presence in the Geraldverse fractured the established order, causing paradoxes, breaking prophecies, and leading to what is now referred to as the Fate-Breaking Incident—a singularity event where multiple predestined timelines collapsed simultaneously, leaving the future of the Geraldverse uncertain for the first time in eternity.

The Overpowered "Cheat Skills" of a Summoned Gerald
Like all classic isekai protagonists, Gerald was not transported into this world empty-handed. Upon his arrival, he awakened a set of reality-defying powers, abilities so unnaturally overpowered that even the Supreme One has expressed concern.

His abilities include:

1. Infinite Growth Potential (Protagonist's Scaling)
Unlike traditional Geralds, who have fixed limitations based on their origin or divine rank, Isekai Protagonist Gerald has no cap on his power.
He grows stronger exponentially, adapting instantly to defeat any opponent.
The longer he exists in the Geraldverse, the closer he comes to surpassing even its greatest rulers.
2. Plot Armor Manipulation
Impossible events always seem to resolve in his favor, regardless of how dire the circumstances.
He has an unnatural ability to survive situations that should be fatal, from reality collapses to battles against god-killers.
Some theorists suggest that fate itself is rewriting existence around him to ensure he remains alive.
3. The Hero’s Luck (Coincidental Destiny)
Legendary weapons, lost artifacts, and powerful allies always seem to appear at just the right moment.
Even his enemies cannot fully resist the influence of his "protagonist presence"—many feel compelled to either join him, admire him, or hate him irrationally.
4. Reality Override (Unbound by Geraldian Law)
Unlike the Supreme One or other higher Geralds, Isekai Protagonist Gerald is not bound by the laws of the Geraldverse.
He can ignore restrictions placed on lesser beings, bypass multiversal barriers, and even rewrite established lore through sheer force of narrative momentum.
A Universe That Fears Its Own Hero
While his unmatched potential has allowed him to survive in the chaotic Geraldverse, it has also made him a universal threat. Many factions view his existence as an aberration, a dangerous anomaly that must be contained or eliminated before he disrupts reality itself.

Enemies of Isekai Protagonist Gerald
The Supreme One – Views Gerald as an unpredictable force that could destabilize the entire multiverse.
The Gerald Corporation – Fears that his unchecked growth could overwrite established Geraldian hierarchy, making traditional power structures irrelevant.
The Enforcers of True Geraldian Lore – Have classified him as an "existential hazard", deploying specialized teams to monitor and, if necessary, neutralize him.
Gerald Prime-1X, the Usurper – Believes Gerald's power belongs to him, and will stop at nothing to claim it.
Allies of Isekai Protagonist Gerald
Rekkan, the Fallen Guardian – A rogue warrior who sees Gerald’s fight against fate as a struggle worth supporting.
Vael, the Exiled Magister – Fascinated by the impossibility of Gerald’s existence, believing he may be the key to unlocking hidden cosmic truths.
Mother Gerald – Protects him like a lost child, sensing that his journey is one of cosmic significance.
Destiny or Freedom? The Question of Self-Will
Though his strength rivals gods, and his luck ensures his continued survival, Isekai Protagonist Gerald is not free from existential doubt. Unlike other Geralds, who accept their roles in the grand order of things, he questions whether he truly has free will—or if he is merely playing out a script written by forces beyond his understanding.

Every encounter, every challenge, every impossible triumph—was it truly his choice?

Or was he simply another cog in a cosmic machine, one whose role was to fulfill a predetermined "protagonist arc"?

Unlike the other Geraldian titans, who battle for supremacy over the multiverse, Isekai Protagonist Gerald seeks something far greater than power. He seeks to break free from destiny itself—to forge a future that belongs to him alone.

Whether he will rise to reshape the Geraldverse, fall to the enemies that seek his erasure, or transcend beyond even the Supreme One, remains unknown.

But one thing is certain—his journey has only just begun.

Valley Girl Gerald – Like, Oh My Gosh, The Most Fabulous Gerald Ever
"Ugh, okay, but like, what even is time? And why is everyone sooo obsessed with, like, multiversal balance? Just chill, babe."

The Most Stylish Gerald in the Geraldverse
In a cosmos filled with omnipotent beings, multiversal bureaucrats, and world-shattering conflicts, Valley Girl Gerald stands out as a beacon of unbothered fabulousness. Where other Geralds concern themselves with power, control, and divine authority, she is far more interested in, like, having a good time, looking amazing, and avoiding literally all unnecessary stress.

Unlike her counterparts, Valley Girl Gerald has zero desire to rule, fight, or engage in any of the tedious nonsense that plagues the Geraldverse. To her, the Supreme One is, like, such a try-hard, and the whole "defend the multiverse" thing is, honestly, kinda cringe. If you ask her, the real meaning of existence is looking cute, sipping overpriced cosmic lattes, and giving unsolicited fashion advice to beings of incomprehensible power.

Origins – Like, How Did She Even Get Here?
The exact origins of Valley Girl Gerald are, like, sooo unclear, mostly because she doesn’t remember and literally does not care. Some theorists claim she was born from a cosmic convergence of glamor and indifference, while others believe she was a failed experiment by the High Overseers to create the "perfectly non-threatening Gerald."

There are also rumors that she wasn't even supposed to exist, but some reality-altering event (probably, like, a total oopsie) accidentally inserted her into the Geraldverse. And since, like, ugh, deleting an entire existence is such a hassle, the higher-ups just kinda… let her stay.

Abilities – Like, Totally OP But in a Chill Way
Despite her carefree nature, Valley Girl Gerald is weirdly overpowered in ways that make no sense, but nobody can really do anything about it because, like, she just doesn't take anything seriously enough to be affected by normal logic.

1. Passive Reality Manipulation (The Power of Vibes)
Valley Girl Gerald doesn’t intend to bend reality—it just, like, happens around her.
If she doesn’t want to deal with something, it ceases to be her problem.
Enemies about to attack her? They just forget why they were mad.
Cosmic crisis? Someone else will totally handle it.
The multiverse just goes along with whatever she wants because it’s easier than trying to fight her lack of concern.
2. Temporal Detachment (Time? Ew.)
Time literally does not affect her.
Deadlines, aging, multiversal collapses—they just don’t apply to her.
If she’s running late? Time adjusts itself to her schedule.
If someone tries to erase her from existence? She just doesn’t acknowledge it, so it doesn’t work.
3. The Like, Ultimate Social Influence (Charisma: 1000)
Everyone somehow ends up liking her, even if they, like, totally didn’t want to.
Entire cosmic factions have changed their policies just because she convinced them it was, like, way more chill to do so.
She has single-handedly negotiated peace treaties by distracting warlords with gossip.
4. Fashion Sense Beyond Mortal Understanding
Her outfits are always flawless, no matter the conditions.
Even in the middle of a collapsing dimension, her hair remains perfectly styled.
She once critiqued the Supreme One’s robes, and instead of being offended, he actually changed them.
Relationships in the Geraldverse – Who’s, Like, Totally Obsessed With Her?
Besties:
Sexy Gerald – They are literally inseparable. The ultimate hot power duo of the Geraldverse.
Mother Gerald – Always calls Valley Girl Gerald her little star, even though she never listens to advice.
Isekai Protagonist Gerald – He has so much main character angst but, like, ugh, she kinda finds it endearing.
People Who Think She’s a Problem (So Rude!):
The Gerald Corporation – They have no idea how she keeps breaking multiversal protocol, but she just, like, does.
The Temporal Compliance Division – They have given up trying to make her follow time laws.
Gerald-X404, the Glitched One – He totally freaks her out. Ew.
The Ultimate Question: What Even Is Her Purpose?
Unlike other Geralds, who have grand destinies and cosmic responsibilities, Valley Girl Gerald just kinda… exists. And yet, the multiverse refuses to function properly without her presence.

Some theorists suggest that she is a fundamental counterbalance to the overly serious chaos of the Geraldverse—a necessary force of apathy and aesthetic perfection that keeps everything from, like, getting too cringe.

But if you ask her? She’ll just, like, shrug, sip her latte, and say:

"Babe, why are you even stressing? Just, like, live your best life, okay?"

Skill Issue Gerald – Why Is He Even Here
"Bro, that was, like, totally not my fault. The universe is just rigged against me."

The Gerald Who Just Can’t Catch a Break
In a multiverse filled with godlike Geralds, reality-breaking anomalies, and cosmic-scale bureaucrats, Skill Issue Gerald is… well, not one of them. Unlike his counterparts, who wield power beyond mortal comprehension, Skill Issue Gerald is spectacularly bad at everything he tries. He isn’t weak—he just has the worst luck imaginable, making him the absolute joke of the Geraldverse.

No matter what he attempts, something always goes catastrophically wrong. If he tries to cast a spell? It backfires horribly. If he tries to fight? He trips on his own sword. If he tries to escape danger? He somehow runs directly into it. Every failure is met with the same resigned sigh from the High Overseers:

"Another skill issue."

And yet, despite his absolute lack of competence, Skill Issue Gerald is somehow still alive, proving that sheer dumb luck is just as powerful as actual skill.

Origins – The Cosmic Joke of the Geraldverse
Nobody really knows where Skill Issue Gerald came from, but most agree that he probably wasn’t meant to exist. Some theorists suggest he was a failed prototype of a perfect Gerald, while others believe he accidentally glitched into reality, much like Gerald-X404.

There’s also a theory that he was once an incredibly powerful Gerald who, due to some horrific multiversal accident, lost all of his abilities and became a walking skill issue instead. Whatever the case, he’s stuck like this now, fumbling his way through existence in the most embarrassing ways possible.

Abilities – If You Can Call Them That
While most Geralds have reality-warping abilities, divine power, or godlike intelligence, Skill Issue Gerald has… something.

1. Cosmic-Level Failure (Passive)
The moment he tries to do anything remotely impressive, it immediately goes wrong.
His magic always backfires, his weapons break, and his plans fall apart in real-time.
Even things that should be impossible to mess up still go horribly wrong.
2. Negative Luck (Skill Issue Manifestation)
If there is a 1% chance of something failing, it will happen to him.
He once tried to sit in a chair and somehow still missed.
If he’s given a weapon of absolute power, it will malfunction at the worst possible moment.
3. Accidental Invincibility (Plot Armor?)
Despite his constant failures, he somehow never dies.
He once fell into a black hole and just… bounced out.
Even the Supreme One himself gave up trying to erase him, because every attempt somehow failed.
4. Inability to Learn (True Skill Issue)
No matter how many times he fails, he never improves.
Training does nothing. Studying does nothing. He is simply bad at everything.
He once had a 1,000-year mentorship with a legendary swordmaster, and at the end of it, he still held his sword backwards.
Relationships in the Geraldverse
People Who Feel Bad for Him:
Mother Gerald – She keeps trying to help him, but, like, it never works.
Valley Girl Gerald – She, like, literally does not understand how someone can be this bad at life.
People Who Mock Him Relentlessly:
Sexy Gerald – "Babe, that’s, like, so embarrassing. I literally can’t watch."
The High Overseers of Gerald Management – They gave up trying to assign him a purpose because, like, why even bother?
Gerald-Ω, the Aberrant Singularity – Even a reality-breaking paradox thinks he’s a joke.
People Who Accidentally Made Him Worse:
The Temporal Compliance Division – Tried to "fix" his skill issue with time manipulation. Somehow made it even worse.
The Enforcers of True Geraldian Lore – Tried to train him. It didn’t work.
The Ultimate Question: Why Is He Even Here?
Despite being the worst Gerald to ever exist, Skill Issue Gerald remains a permanent fixture in the Geraldverse. Some believe he is a necessary cosmic balance, ensuring that not all Geralds are overpowered gods. Others think he exists purely for comedic effect, as a reminder that even among divine beings, failure is still possible.

One thing is for sure: no matter what happens, he will continue to be a walking disaster.

Joel, The 7TV Emote
Joel, The 7TV Emote, is a Gerald whose existence is deeply intertwined with the world of 7TV, a highly influential and ever-evolving emote platform known for its unique, bizarre, and sometimes chaotic contributions to internet culture. Though he lacks the cosmic power of many Geralds, Joel’s identity is built upon the backbone of memes, emotes, and the vibrant, sometimes erratic 7TV community. He is not just an emote; he is a living embodiment of 7TV's atmosphere: constantly shifting, always reacting, and fully immersed in the vibrant, meme-laden world of modern digital interaction.

Joel came into being through the confluence of internet culture and the innovative power of 7TV emotes, becoming the personification of the community-driven and constantly changing meme world. His form and powers reflect the creativity and absurdity that 7TV represents, making him a Gerald unlike any other.

Origins of Joel
Joel’s creation is a tale of digital transformation. Unlike the more traditional Geralds who are born from cosmic events or divine birthrights, Joel emerged as a byproduct of a strange phenomenon within the 7TV platform. 7TV was a place where unique, sometimes strange emotes could be shared, used, and evolved. Joel’s birth is said to have occurred when a particularly popular, ever-changing emote on 7TV suddenly gained sentience—a combination of memes, digital energy, and the collective thoughts of internet users who shared and loved it.

It is said that one night, as 7TV servers were overloaded with meme data, Joel somehow broke free from the digital realm, becoming an entity unto himself. Unlike other Geralds, who exist outside or above specific digital cultures, Joel’s being is entirely intertwined with the 7TV ecosystem, making him uniquely susceptible to the fluctuations and transformations of the internet’s meme culture.

He was born to express emotions in the form of 7TV emotes—his face constantly shifting and contorting into different, expressive forms. At first, his identity was no more than a glitch in the system, but as time passed, Joel grew into a self-aware, independent Gerald with the ability to fully interact with the world around him.

Appearance and Traits
Joel's appearance is an ever-changing, chaotic blend of 7TV emote faces, with each one capturing the full range of emotions that internet users experience online. These expressions are not simply cosmetic but are integral to his powers and interactions with others in the Geraldverse. His face shifts between various well-known 7TV emotes, each of which he can manifest physically and bring to life in the world around him.

PeepoSmile: Joel’s most iconic expression—a wide, goofy grin that represents unbridled joy and carefree laughter. This expression is often seen when Joel is in a playful mood or trying to lighten the mood around him.
FeelsGoodMan: This emote is used by Joel to express feelings of happiness and satisfaction, usually when he has pulled off something particularly clever or when a situation has turned out in his favor.
PeepoSad: A sorrowful expression, used by Joel to convey moments of melancholy or when a situation becomes too absurd or frustrating for even him to handle. His face droops, and his eyes water slightly.
MonkaS: Joel’s face contorts into a look of anxiety or nervousness, which he uses in tense or stressful moments. When something ominous or unsettling happens, the MonkaS face emerges, signaling a disturbance in the atmosphere.
Pogger: The face of surprise, excitement, and amazement. Joel uses this face when something incredible or shocking happens, representing those "wow" moments that trigger massive reactions.
LULW: Joel’s face twists into a laughing expression, used to signify pure, unbridled amusement at the absurdity of life or the things happening around him. This emote shows Joel in his most carefree, comedic form.
FeelsDankMan: An expression of deep internet culture immersion, used by Joel when he experiences or creates moments that are deeply tied to meme history or internet subcultures.
These faces are not just emotes; they are living embodiments of Joel’s emotional energy. When Joel adopts a particular face or emote, he can alter the mood or atmosphere of the world around him. Each emote has a unique cosmic resonance that can affect those who interact with it, often bending their perceptions, emotions, or even behaviors. For example, Joel's PeepoSmile may bring an unexpected wave of happiness to those nearby, while his MonkaS face could induce anxiety or fear.

Joel's body, much like his facial expressions, is fluid and not fixed. It changes based on what internet meme or subculture is at the forefront of the 7TV community. One moment, he might wear a hoodie with the “Poggers” logo emblazoned on the front, and the next, he might sport an outfit based on the “Cursed” meme or “Pepe” variations. His appearance evolves in real-time as meme culture shifts, constantly mirroring the trends and waves that come and go.

Abilities
Joel’s powers are drawn from the digital energy of 7TV itself, and as such, they are primarily centered around meme manipulation, emotion control, and reality distortion.

Emote Projection: Joel can project any 7TV emote into the physical world, creating real versions of these digital expressions. For example, he might summon a MonkaS figure that reflects the collective anxiety of a situation or create a FeelsDankMan entity to symbolize the depth of an emotional experience. These projections can interact with reality and can even influence the emotions of those they come into contact with.
Meme Reality Manipulation: Joel has the ability to warp reality itself through the power of memes. His presence can cause subtle but significant distortions, turning everyday objects into viral references or altering the flow of time and events based on how memes operate within the Geraldverse. If a meme becomes popular enough, Joel can bring it to life, creating meme-based anomalies that function as real entities within the multiverse.
Stream Power: Drawing power from the endless stream of content that circulates through the 7TV network, Joel can tap into the collective digital energy of the platform. The more attention he garners from internet communities, the stronger his abilities become. This includes gaining heightened senses, enhanced reaction speed, and increased meme manipulation power the more “views” or engagement he receives.
Glitching: As a being born from a network filled with endless data streams, Joel can create minor glitches in the fabric of reality. These glitches take the form of temporary visual distortions, stuttering time loops, or distorted spatial pockets, often leaving behind a surreal, chaotic effect wherever they appear. These glitches often create moments of absurdity or unexpected shifts in behavior, aligning with the randomness and unpredictability of the digital world.
Digital Personality Projection: One of Joel’s more fascinating abilities is the power to project personalities based on internet trends or Twitch streamers. This allows him to temporarily embody the personality of a famous figure in the online world, adapting to their specific mannerisms, speech patterns, and behaviors. This ability is often used for both comedic effect and to create moments of internet chaos.
Personality
Joel is, above all else, a creature of internet culture. His personality is a bizarre mix of humor, sarcasm, and chaotic energy. He is playful, quick-witted, and thrives in environments of social interaction and digital connection. Joel’s primary motivations are to entertain, disrupt, and engage with the world around him—much like the memes and emotes he represents.

He can be self-serving and often enjoys making light of serious situations, using his emotes to distort reality and provoke laughter. However, he also possesses a deep understanding of the internet’s power—he knows that memes are not just tools of amusement, but also powerful vehicles of emotion and influence. Despite his sometimes absurd antics, Joel understands that he is part of a larger digital ecosystem—one that shapes modern culture, communication, and connection.

Joel’s charm lies in his unpredictability and his ability to shift between emotional states. He can go from pure comedic relief to deep digital reflection, often drawing from the memes and trends that resonate most with internet users. This emotional fluidity makes him an enigmatic yet deeply relatable figure for those familiar with the rapid changes of the internet.

Legacy
Joel, though never a central figure in the grand schemes of the Geraldverse, has carved out a unique and powerful role for himself. His existence as a 7TV emote symbol has made him a cultural icon—one that is passed around between the multiverses as a reminder of the chaotic beauty of internet culture. His legacy is a reminder that even in a universe full of grand cosmic battles and immense power struggles, sometimes the most influential figure is one who simply reflects the absurdity and joy that the digital age has to offer.

In the Geraldverse, Joel stands as the meme trickster, a reminder that while reality may be serious and overwhelming, the best way to survive it is to laugh, meme, and keep scrolling.

Crusty Gerald, The Forgotten One
Crusty Gerald is a Gerald whose existence and appearance are deeply tied to the forgotten corners of the Geraldverse—the places where memories fade, and time itself becomes a bit too aged to remember. Born from the decay of old digital entities and the passing of forgotten memes, Crusty Gerald embodies everything that has been neglected, left behind, and forsaken. His form is both a physical manifestation of time’s toll and a reminder that even in the vast multiverse of Geralds, there are those who have outlived their relevance and been discarded into obscurity.

Origins of Crusty Gerald
Crusty Gerald’s creation is tied to a failed experiment within the Gerald Management System—an attempt to revitalize a long-dead version of a Gerald that had outlived its usefulness. Originally, Crusty Gerald was a clean, pristine Gerald who had been part of the Prime Gerald Family, a noble lineage meant to uphold the order of the Geraldverse. However, as time went on, this Gerald began to lose favor among the more powerful Geralds, slowly fading from memory as newer, flashier versions emerged.

The experiment began as an effort to reintroduce relevance to the forgotten Gerald, but something went wrong. Instead of revitalizing him, the process left him in a state of dilapidation, both physically and metaphysically. Crusty Gerald’s body became warped and cracked, his form a collection of rotting matter and fractured existence, almost as if he were a relic of an era that should have stayed buried. His consciousness became clouded by a sense of nostalgia for his former self, and he wandered the multiverse as a symbol of the decay of forgotten time.

The once-pristine Gerald now roams aimlessly, often found in forgotten places, sitting in the corner of abandoned realms, or watching as other Geralds rise and fall. While he may not possess the cosmic power that many Geralds wield, Crusty Gerald represents something else entirely: a force that reminds others that nothing lasts forever, not even the mighty Geraldverse.

Appearance and Traits
Crusty Gerald’s appearance reflects his forgotten nature. His skin is cracked and faded, resembling the texture of moss-covered stone, aged parchment, and decaying wood. His once vibrant colors are now muted, and his eyes have a glazed, hollow look, as though he’s perpetually stuck between the realms of memory and oblivion. Dirt, dust, and grime seem to be part of his very being, accumulating as he travels through time and space, leaving a trail of gritty particles behind him.

His clothing is a patchwork of old, torn garments, each one representing a past era or forgotten memory. His cloak, once fine and regal, now appears to be shredded and stained with ancient stains—a visual metaphor for his decaying existence. Vines, fungi, and moss seem to cling to him, as though he’s become part of the landscape of forgotten time, with a faint smell of earth and rot emanating from him.

Despite his physical decay, Crusty Gerald retains a certain dignity in his stance. He walks slowly and purposefully, as if each step is a reminder of the weight of the passing ages. His voice, when he speaks, is rough and gravelly, as though it hasn’t been used in eons. Crusty Gerald doesn’t communicate often, but when he does, his words are laced with melancholy, reminding others of the impermanence of time.

Abilities
Crusty Gerald may appear to be a weak and forgotten figure, but his abilities are rooted in the aging and decay of time itself. His powers are subtle, often relying on the natural forces of entropy, memory, and nostalgia.

Decay of Time: Crusty Gerald has the ability to influence the passage of time within a localized area. With a mere touch or a glance, he can age objects and decay structures, causing them to crumble into ruin. This ability reflects his nature as the embodiment of all things forgotten and left behind, and it is especially potent in places where time has been left unchecked.
Memory Degradation: One of Crusty Gerald’s most terrifying powers is his ability to erase memories. When he makes contact with another being, he can slowly drain their memories, causing them to forget their purpose, identity, or even their past lives. This power feeds on the concept of obsolescence—the more a memory is ignored or neglected, the more susceptible it becomes to Crusty Gerald’s influence.
Erosion Aura: Those who come into close contact with Crusty Gerald are affected by his eroding presence. His very being radiates an aura that causes the environment around him to deteriorate—grass turns to dust, buildings crumble, and even the air seems to grow thicker and harder to breathe. This power reflects the slow decay of everything in the universe, reinforcing the idea that nothing is permanent, no matter how mighty it once was.
Echoes of the Forgotten: Crusty Gerald can summon the echoes of lost memories and long-forgotten entities. These echoes appear as ghostly figures, voices in the wind, or distorted whispers that call out to those who have forgotten certain truths. They can create confusion, disorientation, and sometimes even visions of the past, showing things that should have remained forgotten.
The Weight of Time: Crusty Gerald can temporarily impose the weight of ages upon others. By merely glancing at someone or making brief contact, he can inflict a time-based curse that makes the target feel the weight of millennia, as if their body has aged beyond its years. This causes immense physical and emotional strain, as well as a growing sense of lost purpose.
Reverse Nostalgia: In a twisted reversal of traditional nostalgia, Crusty Gerald can evoke feelings of regret and sorrow in those around him. Rather than longing for the past in a hopeful way, those affected by Crusty Gerald’s power feel a deep sadness and frustration over the passage of time, as if the things they once cherished have been irrevocably lost. This often causes people to question their own existence and whether they are destined to fade away like the many forgotten things that Crusty Gerald represents.
Personality
Crusty Gerald’s personality is deeply shaped by his forgotten nature. He is not malicious, but neither is he benevolent. He is, above all else, a being of quiet sorrow—a reminder that all things eventually decay and fade away, no matter how significant they once seemed. His speech is infrequent, but when he does speak, it is usually in riddles or cryptic phrases that reveal the fragility of existence.

He holds a melancholic wisdom, understanding that everything—power, time, even the Geralds themselves—is subject to the inevitable passage of time. Crusty Gerald does not actively seek to destroy or disrupt, but rather exists as a quiet observer of the decay and inevitable passing of all things.

There are moments when Crusty Gerald’s wisdom shines through, revealing a deeper understanding of the ebb and flow of the universe. He is not angry at being forgotten; instead, he accepts it as a natural part of the cycle. He is neither a hero nor a villain—he simply exists, fading from memory like the things he represents.

Legacy
Crusty Gerald’s legacy is a quiet one, but no less profound. He is the embodiment of the forgotten, the lost, and the decayed—a reminder that time moves forward, and nothing remains static. In the vast multiverse, where Geralds rise and fall, Crusty Gerald is a figure of nostalgia, inevitability, and acceptance.

Though he may not play a central role in the great events of the Geraldverse, his influence is felt by those who dwell in forgotten realms or those who feel lost in time. Crusty Gerald stands as a figure that encourages others to reflect on the passing of time and the finiteness of their own existence—an eternal symbol that, no matter how grand, everything must eventually return to dust.

In the end, Crusty Gerald reminds all who encounter him that nothing lasts forever—not even the most powerful or beloved Geralds.

Cooking Gerald, He Who Cooks
In the vast and ever-expanding Geraldverse, a curious yet deeply revered figure stands out—Cooking Gerald, known far and wide as He Who Cooks. He is a master of culinary arts, a conjurer of flavors, and a bearer of dishes so divine they can alter the fabric of reality itself. Where most Geralds wield power over time, space, and existence, Cooking Gerald wields the timeless and universal art of cooking. His realm is one where ingredients blend to form not only sustenance but also gateways, solutions, and sometimes, pure transcendence. A simple meal made by his hand can change the course of a battle, heal broken hearts, and even offer revelations about the very nature of the multiverse.

Origins of Cooking Gerald
The origins of Cooking Gerald are shrouded in mystery, as is the case with many Geralds. Some believe that he was once a humble mortal who simply loved to cook, becoming so skilled that he eventually transcended his human limitations, gaining the ability to manipulate the very essence of ingredients and flavors to alter the world around him. Others claim that he was born of a cosmic rift—an anomaly in the Geraldverse that sought to merge the physical, the metaphysical, and the gastronomical. However, regardless of the truth, one thing is certain: Cooking Gerald’s skills are unparalleled, and his meals are said to possess powers that extend far beyond ordinary cooking.

Cooking Gerald’s kitchen is not confined to a conventional space—rather, it exists in a pocket dimension where all ingredients are sourced from the infinite multiverses. His cooking utensils are rumored to be enchanted, capable of creating anything from simple dishes to meals capable of altering perceptions of reality. He is a figure known both for his culinary expertise and for his ability to manipulate the forces of the Geraldverse through his meals.

Appearance and Traits
Cooking Gerald’s appearance is as unique as his abilities. Unlike the pristine and sometimes austere appearance of other Geralds, Cooking Gerald is often seen wearing a chef’s apron, covered in splatters of various cosmic sauces, mystical spices, and ethereal oils. His clothes are practical but always carry an air of understated elegance—a simple white shirt, comfy pants, and chef's hat that somehow always seems to stay immaculate despite the culinary chaos that surrounds him.

His face carries a calm, almost serene expression, but his eyes have a spark of passion and creativity that few others can match. His skin, usually a slightly golden hue, seems to radiate warmth, as though he is always surrounded by the smell of freshly baked bread or simmering stew. Cooking Gerald’s most noticeable feature, however, is the faint, ever-present scent of deliciousness that seems to follow him wherever he goes—a mix of herbs, spices, and rich broths that stir both hunger and awe.

Despite his culinary prowess, Cooking Gerald does not see himself as a mere chef. He is a creator and an alchemist—each meal he prepares is an act of creation, capable of manifesting not only flavor but also deep, intrinsic truths about the world and the people who eat his food.

Abilities
Cooking Gerald’s abilities transcend the ordinary realms of cooking and enter into the cosmic, mystical, and existential. What makes Cooking Gerald truly unique is his ability to infuse his creations with powers that reach beyond the mere act of nourishment. These abilities include:

Cosmic Cuisine: The ability to create dishes that tap into the very fundamentals of the universe. By combining rare ingredients and spices harvested from across the multiverse, Cooking Gerald can create meals that manipulate time, alter memories, or even temporarily shift realities. For instance, a simple bowl of soup could slow time for a single person, or a fruit salad could restore a fractured soul.
Gastronomical Transmutation: Cooking Gerald can transmute one substance into another through the use of his culinary mastery. For example, he can turn a humble slice of bread into a gateway to another realm or change water into a healing elixir. This ability comes not from magic but from an inherent understanding of the true nature of ingredients and how they connect to the fabric of the multiverse.
Flavor Manipulation: Beyond the physical properties of food, Cooking Gerald can manipulate the emotional and psychological responses of those who consume his meals. With a perfectly cooked dish, he can invoke feelings of nostalgia, love, or even peace, helping people confront deep emotions. Conversely, his creations can also draw out hidden desires, fears, or even memories long buried—allowing him to subtly influence others through their senses.
Infusion of Power: Cooking Gerald has the rare ability to infuse his food with the power of the Geraldverse itself. By adding specific ingredients or cooking them in a particular way, he can create dishes that grant temporary boosts in power, speed, or intellect. This power is limited, however, as each dish can only be imbued with enough power to influence the immediate moment rather than causing lasting changes.
Culinary Summoning: With the right ingredients, Cooking Gerald can summon entities or manifest creatures from other realms to assist in his work or to serve his guests. These creations are often temporary, lasting only for as long as the meal is being consumed or until the food's purpose has been fulfilled.
Kitchen Manifestation: Cooking Gerald’s kitchen is an ever-shifting, multi-dimensional space. He can summon ingredients and tools from any corner of the Geraldverse, and his culinary creations appear in pocket dimensions where they are protected from outside forces. This space is described as an unholy blend of traditional kitchens, ethereal gardens, and exotic marketplaces where he can source anything his recipes require, from cosmic fruits to stardust.
Ultimate Meal of Truth: Cooking Gerald’s final dish—a legendary meal known as the "Eternal Feast"—is said to reveal the deepest truths about the one who consumes it. The meal can unlock a person’s true potential, show them their fate, or even change the course of their entire life. This dish is said to have been crafted only once, and its true recipe is kept a closely guarded secret. Only those deemed worthy will ever be served this ultimate meal.
Personality
Despite his immense power, Cooking Gerald is surprisingly humble, always eager to share his creations with others. His passion for cooking is matched only by his love for seeing people satisfied and nourished—both physically and spiritually. He is kind, generous, and highly attuned to the needs and desires of others. His calm demeanor is often paired with a playful wit, as he enjoys teaching others the art of cooking and sharing his knowledge of the universe’s deeper culinary secrets.

However, Cooking Gerald is not without his quirks. He is extremely particular about his ingredients, and no matter the cosmic event occurring around him, he is always searching for the perfect seasoning or fresh herb. His belief in the power of food as a bridge between worlds and a conduit for truth can make him somewhat zealous at times, but his intentions are always pure—after all, his greatest joy comes from bringing people together through the act of eating.

Legacy
Cooking Gerald is a figure beloved across the multiverse. In many realms, he is seen as a symbol of hope, a figure that transcends the power struggles and cosmic conflicts that dominate the Geraldverse. His meals bring peace, understanding, and unity to those who partake in them, and he has become a sought-after figure among those looking to find clarity in their own existence.

Legends tell of times when the Geralds of old have gathered around his tables, setting aside their cosmic differences to enjoy a meal and, for once, not battle for power, but simply exist in harmony. Cooking Gerald’s greatest legacy, though, remains the meal of truth, an offering that holds the key to unlocking not just personal growth but a deeper understanding of the multiverse itself.

Thus, Cooking Gerald remains a beloved and revered figure, who, through the magic of food, continues to leave a lasting impact on the multiverse, proving that in the face of chaos, sometimes the greatest power lies in a simple meal shared in good company.

Sadge Gerald, The Depressed One
In a multiverse of infinite possibilities, where countless versions of Gerald roam and shape the fabric of reality, there exists a Gerald who stands as the embodiment of melancholia and sorrow. Known simply as Sadge Gerald, or more solemnly as The Depressed One, this version of Gerald is marked by an overwhelming sense of existential despair, hopelessness, and emotional turmoil. His very presence seems to carry a palpable weight, as though he is burdened by the sheer futility of existence. He is the walking, talking manifestation of a cosmic crisis of the soul, a Gerald whose very essence is defined by an ongoing internal battle with himself and the world around him.

Origins of Sadge Gerald
The origins of Sadge Gerald are steeped in mystery, much like many other versions of Gerald who exist across the multiverse. Some theories suggest that Sadge Gerald was the product of a catastrophic emotional breakdown, a result of experiencing too many cosmic realities, each more painful and confusing than the last. Others believe that he was born of a world that had long since lost hope, where every possible victory was overshadowed by an impending sense of futility.

There is also speculation that Sadge Gerald was the result of an experiment gone wrong—an attempt to create a Gerald who could understand and sympathize with the unbearable nature of existence. Whether by choice or accident, this Gerald became more attuned to the darker, bleaker aspects of life, finding meaning only in the pain and sadness that seemed to haunt him at every turn. He wandered the realms in search of solace but never found it, instead constantly drowning in an ocean of self-doubt, regret, and an overwhelming sense of pointlessness.

Appearance and Traits
Unlike other more radiant or powerful versions of Gerald, Sadge Gerald’s appearance is marked by his somber demeanor. His posture is often hunched, as though carrying an invisible weight. His face is drawn and tired, with dark circles under his eyes and an overall dull, colorless appearance that reflects his inner turmoil. His expression rarely changes—it's as if a cloud of sadness has permanently settled over him, one that is almost impossible to lift.

Sadge Gerald’s clothing is often dark and unremarkable—typically consisting of loose, unkempt garments that seem to further highlight his lack of interest in the world around him. His eyes, usually a dull, almost lifeless shade of gray, seem to hold a deep sorrow, a void that he’s never been able to fill. His hair is often messy, falling in unkempt strands over his face, and he has a tendency to avoid direct eye contact with others, as though ashamed of his own existence.

Abilities
Though his powers are not as grandiose or impressive as other versions of Gerald, Sadge Gerald’s abilities are still deeply tied to his melancholic existence. His powers often manifest in ways that mirror his emotional state, creating subtle yet impactful effects in the environments and people around him. His abilities include:

Aura of Despair: Sadge Gerald exudes an aura that causes emotional decay in those around him. Anyone who comes into contact with him will begin to feel an overwhelming sense of sadness, helplessness, and self-doubt. It’s as if being near him is a constant reminder of the inevitability of loss and the fragility of hope. This power does not manifest as overt aggression but rather as an insidious, quiet collapse of morale.
Illusions of Hopelessness: Due to his emotional turmoil, Sadge Gerald has the ability to create illusions that reflect his own internal sadness. These illusions often take the form of nightmarish visions of failure, loss, and betrayal. Those who fall victim to these illusions are trapped in cycles of despair, reliving their worst moments or imagining their most feared outcomes, unable to escape the overwhelming sense of futility.
Reality Dissociation: Sadge Gerald has the unique ability to distort reality around him based on his emotional state. In moments of extreme sadness or emotional breakdown, the environment around him may distort—colors may fade, landscapes may become barren, and the laws of nature might seem to slow down or become chaotic. This effect is largely passive but powerful, causing those near him to question the stability of the world and their place within it.
Empathy of Suffering: Unlike most Geralds, who can inflict pain or wield power with force, Sadge Gerald has the rare ability to feel the pain and sorrow of others. This power allows him to connect with others on a deeply emotional level, but it also drains him. By absorbing the negative emotions of those around him, he becomes more in tune with their suffering, but at the cost of his own mental and emotional well-being.
Eternal Weeping: In moments of extreme sorrow or emotional upheaval, Sadge Gerald can summon tears that are said to possess the power to cleanse or taint depending on the nature of his weeping. These tears can heal wounds, but the emotional price is high—those who are healed by them often feel an overwhelming sense of loss or loneliness, as though the healing came at the expense of their connection to others.
Melancholic Manipulation: Sadge Gerald has the ability to manipulate sounds and vibrations around him, creating an atmosphere filled with mournful, sorrowful noises. These might manifest as haunting melodies, distant crying, or echoes of lost voices. The sound of despair that emanates from him has the power to deeply affect anyone who hears it, leaving them feeling melancholic and unmotivated.
Personality
Sadge Gerald is defined by his profound sadness and his inability to find peace within himself. He is introverted and often avoids interaction with others, feeling disconnected from the world around him. His thoughts are often consumed by the belief that life is futile, and that no matter what actions he takes, nothing will ever improve. This has caused him to retreat inward, focusing on his own sense of despair rather than seeking external solutions.

Though deeply melancholic, Sadge Gerald is not malevolent. He does not wish harm on others; rather, he is simply overwhelmed by the feeling that all things, including himself, are meaningless. His empathy for others' suffering is unmatched, yet he often feels as though he is unworthy of their sympathy. He tends to push people away, either out of fear of becoming a burden or out of belief that they would ultimately abandon him once they see the full depth of his sorrow.

Despite his tragic nature, there are moments when Sadge Gerald shows glimmers of hope—brief flickers where he dreams of a world where he might finally find peace or understanding. These moments are fleeting, and just as quickly as they appear, they are lost in the swirling fog of his depression. However, it is this faint glimmer of hope that keeps him moving forward, even if he believes it is nothing more than an illusion.

Legacy
Sadge Gerald is often seen as a tragic figure within the Geraldverse, a reminder of the weight of existence and the unavoidable nature of suffering. While other Geralds strive for power, control, or personal glory, Sadge Gerald remains a solemn figure—a witness to the inner battles that rage in every being, even the seemingly all-powerful Geralds. He is both a reflection and a warning: that no matter how great or powerful one may be, they are never immune to the weight of despair.

In the Geraldverse, his name is spoken with reverence and sadness, not for his power, but for the depth of his sadness. Legends say that those who encounter Sadge Gerald often walk away with a new understanding of their own emotions, as though meeting him opens the door to their own vulnerabilities. In his sorrow, he teaches others the value of empathy and the importance of acknowledging and facing the darker parts of existence.

In the end, Sadge Gerald remains a figure of melancholy—a paradox of sadness within a universe filled with unimaginable potential and chaos. Though he may never find solace, his story serves as a reminder that even in the darkest moments, existence is still worth living, if only for the briefest, fleeting glimpse of peace.Freaky Gerald
In a multiverse as vast and chaotic as the Geraldverse, where each version of Gerald holds unique qualities, there exists one that defies all expectations and shatters the very concept of "normal." Known simply as Freaky Gerald, this particular version of Gerald is an unpredictable force of nature, characterized by his bizarre, unsettling presence and penchant for embracing the most outlandish behaviors and appearances. From his twisted, constantly shifting form to his eccentric actions, Freaky Gerald thrives in the realm of chaos and disorder, fully embracing the weird and the unnerving.

Origins of Freaky Gerald
The origins of Freaky Gerald remain shrouded in mystery, but one prevailing theory suggests that he was birthed from a glitch in the Geraldverse itself—a corruption in the fabric of reality that gave rise to a Gerald who was not bound by the traditional laws of logic or structure. Rather than existing in a predictable state, Freaky Gerald's very essence seems to fluctuate at random, constantly morphing into new forms, adopting new behaviors, and playing by a set of unwritten rules that no one but him understands.

Another theory suggests that Freaky Gerald is the product of an experiment gone wrong, where a group of powerful Geralds sought to create a being who could manipulate the fabric of existence itself. However, the experiment went awry, and the result was a Gerald who existed beyond the constraints of reason, embracing the absurd and the strangely wonderful.

Regardless of his origins, Freaky Gerald has come to embody unpredictability, chaos, and an insatiable thirst for the bizarre. Where other Geralds strive for order or power, Freaky Gerald's goal is simply to revel in the oddity of existence.

Appearance
Freaky Gerald's appearance is in constant flux, reflecting his inherent chaos and unpredictability. He has no fixed form—his features can change at will, often warping in ways that defy any logic or standard of beauty. One moment, he might appear as a gargantuan, gelatinous blob, squelching with every movement, while the next, he could transform into an impossibly tall figure with an elongated neck, or a grotesque hybrid of animalistic and humanoid features.

His eyes might shift between colors at random, from glowing red to eerie green to pitch-black, giving him a gaze that unsettles anyone who dares look into them. His limbs might stretch and retract, his mouth may open in unnatural ways, and his voice is known to echo with bizarre frequencies—sometimes high-pitched, sometimes deep, but always unsettling.

Freaky Gerald's appearance is often paired with grotesque or surreal imagery, such as tentacles sprouting from unexpected places, eyes appearing on his body, or mouths that speak in multiple voices. His presence often causes a ripple in reality itself, warping the environment around him in strange ways. Time may slow down, colors may distort, or gravity may no longer apply properly as he walks into a room.

Abilities
Freaky Gerald’s powers are tied to his very essence: unpredictability. He has an incredible ability to warp reality in bizarre, chaotic ways, often with no regard for the laws of physics or logic. Some of his abilities include:

Reality Warping: Freaky Gerald can distort the world around him to suit his whims. This can include altering the laws of physics, shifting dimensions, or even causing objects to defy their intended purpose. The changes he makes are rarely consistent, and they often happen randomly, adding an element of chaos to his very existence.
Shape-Shifting: As mentioned, Freaky Gerald has the ability to change his form at will. His body might transform into different creatures, materials, or even abstract concepts—anything from a smoke cloud to a swarm of insects to a living storm cloud of energy. His shape-shifting abilities are not just limited to his physical form; he can alter his voice, thoughts, and perceptions as well, making him a constantly shifting enigma.
Uncontrollable Moods: Freaky Gerald’s emotional state directly affects the world around him. When he's feeling particularly chaotic, reality itself seems to become unstable, distorting in weird and often disturbing ways. When he’s in a more playful or mischievous mood, his environment may become oddly whimsical, with objects behaving in strange and humorous ways. When he's angry or frustrated, the world around him may begin to warp into nightmarish, grotesque forms.
Inverted Logic: Freaky Gerald can twist logic and reasoning, making situations that would seem impossible suddenly feel entirely normal. This ability allows him to create paradoxes, where the rules of causality and reasoning break down completely. People around him may find themselves trapped in loops or engaging in completely nonsensical conversations, all governed by his whims.
Temporal Distortion: Time, in Freaky Gerald’s presence, does not behave as it does elsewhere. He can cause time to speed up, slow down, or even reverse, leaving those around him in a constant state of disorientation. However, his manipulation of time is rarely precise—it is chaotic, and often causes unintended consequences, such as jumping from one timeline to another or creating rifts between parallel universes.
Emotional Contagion: Freaky Gerald can cause others to experience emotions or moods that match his own. If he’s feeling joyful, those around him may begin to act in silly, carefree ways. If he’s feeling melancholic or anxious, he can impart those emotions onto others, even causing a collective sense of unease that spreads among entire groups. This power only adds to his unpredictability, as he may intentionally or unintentionally cause emotions to escalate into chaotic states.
Absurdist Reality: One of Freaky Gerald’s most dangerous abilities is his power to create absurd worlds where anything is possible, but nothing makes sense. He can generate entire environments where the laws of logic and reasoning no longer apply, leading to surreal experiences where the rules of the universe are replaced with whimsy and absurdity. These worlds might feature gravity-defying buildings, walking trees, or endless loops of nonsense, confusing and disorienting all who step inside.
Personality
Freaky Gerald’s personality is as erratic as his powers. He is playful and mischievous, enjoying chaos for the sake of chaos. He finds humor in disorder, delighting in the confusion he causes and the anomalies he creates. However, his actions are never truly malevolent—he is not out to cause harm or destruction for its own sake. His behavior is more aligned with the idea of fun and absurdity, often just wanting to see what happens if he bends the rules of reality.

Freaky Gerald is also highly curious. He loves exploring new realms, meeting strange beings, and testing the limits of what can be done within the bounds of the Geraldverse. He thrives on the unknown and the unpredictable, and he often enjoys taking risks just to see how far he can push things before something breaks.

At times, Freaky Gerald can be downright unpredictable in his actions, switching between being helpful and destructive depending on his mood or whim. There are moments when he may assist others in their quests, offering strange advice or bizarre tools that could prove useful, and other times, when he might completely derail their plans simply for the amusement of it.

Legacy
Though Freaky Gerald’s presence is often unsettling, his existence has had a lasting impact on the Geraldverse. He serves as a reminder of the inherent chaos that exists within all realities and the unpredictable nature of the multiverse. While many see him as an embodiment of madness, others view him as a symbol of freedom, free from the constraints of logic and order.

Over time, Freaky Gerald has come to be seen as a sort of cosmic trickster, forever dancing at the edges of reason, reminding all who encounter him that sometimes, reality itself can be bent and reshaped into something unrecognizable.

Tbh Creature / Tism Gerald
"Yipee!"
Tbh Creature, also known as Yipee or Yippee, is a quirky and endearing entity that has found a place in the Geraldverse, bringing with it a mix of humor, internet culture, and the charm of simplicity. Originally an MS Paint drawing featuring a white, four-legged creature with a large head, big black eyes, and a neutral expression, the character first made its appearance on Twitter in January 2021. It quickly spread through Tumblr by early 2022, gaining immense popularity and inspiring a whole array of fan art, memes, and jokes. Its sometimes-joking connection to autism and its iconic sound effect, "yipee," has helped it become a symbol of the quirky, offbeat humor that thrives in online spaces.

Origins of Yipee Gerald
Tbh Creature was first created as a simple, minimalist MS Paint character, with its neutral face and large eyes giving it an aura of both innocence and a touch of weirdness. As it began circulating on social media, it was quickly embraced by the internet community, particularly in places like Tumblr where its simple design made it an easy vehicle for memes. The creature’s neutral expression and big eyes, while seemingly emotionless, are part of what makes it so relatable and humorous—its strange, blank stare invites people to project their own feelings and reactions onto it.
